6. **Embedded operationally** in Jersey City to a degree that makes detachment functionally impossible.
7. **Been turned into a symbol used against her own values** (Kamala's Law) and survived without abandoning the values, at the cost of a new and lasting fatigue.

The behavioral micro-signatures acquired in this period — the half-second authority-pause, the right-hand shake-out before embiggening, the amulet-carrying, the speaking-last-in-meetings, the micro-flinch at her own name in official mouths, the notebook continuity device, the refusal to relocate from Jersey — are the durable physical and procedural residue of the middle period and form the operational baseline against which the later period (death, resurrection, mutant reclassification) will be measured.

She enters this period a girl who had survived being unseen. She leaves it a young woman who has survived being *misused while seen*, which is the harder problem and the one she has not yet finished solving.


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# CHRONOLOGY IV — RECENT HISTORY & CURRENT STATE

## Preamble: Period Under Review

This section covers the interval from approximately the immediate post-*Outlawed* aftermath (2021) through the resurrection arc and into the current operating posture: the death in *Amazing Spider-Man* #26 (June 2023), the *Fallen Friend* one-shot (July 2023), the mutant-retcon and Krakoan-protocol resurrection, the *Ms. Marvel: The New Mutant* miniseries (Ahmed, 2023–2024), the *X-Men* main-roster integration under the Krakoa-collapse / "Fall of X" / Orchis crisis, and her status entering the post-Krakoa "From the Ashes" status quo. The throughline of this period — its defining biographical fact — is that the Subject *died young, in front of her parents' household, and came back as a member of a category her parents had not previously had to integrate*. Everything in her current operating state is downstream of that.

## 1. The Late-Adolescent Plateau (Pre-Death Baseline, ~2021–2023)

Coming out of *Outlawed*, the Subject was in a state best described as **convalescent over-functioning**. Kamala's Law had been overturned in practice but had not been psychologically processed; she continued Champions-adjacent activity but with reduced visibility, and the *Beyond* arc reinserted her into Spider-Man's orbit (her brief tenure carrying a Spider-mantle adjacent role, and her warm working rapport with Peter Parker, dates from this window). Granular behavioral markers from the period:

- **College transition.** Subject enrolled at Empire State University, commuting from Jersey City rather than moving to campus dorms — a choice over-determined by (a) family preference, (b) financial pragmatism, (c) her own difficulty leaving the radius of Yusuf, Muneeba, and Aamir. Course load skewed toward writing, comparative literature, and computer science (the latter a Bruno-legacy interest she had absorbed and not abandoned). Her academic record from this period is unremarkable-good: she is a B+ student who could be an A student if she slept.
- **Patrol pattern.** Reduced from the pre-*Outlawed* peak. Where the early Wilson run shows nightly excursions, this period shows a more episodic deployment: weekend nights, response-to-call, and a quiet daytime habit of walking specific corridors of Jersey City (the waterfront, the stretch near the Circle Q, the blocks around her mosque) as ambient situational monitoring rather than active patrol.
- **Relational repair work.** Quiet, undramatized reconciliations with Bruno over text and occasional video calls (he remained in Wakanda for much of this stretch); a deeper integration with Aamir and Tyesha's household — she became a regular babysitter for their child, a role she took with disproportionate seriousness.
- **Affective state.** Subdued but not depressive. The humor was still present but ran drier; the fan-energy register was tempered. Multiple background panels in this era show her drawing or writing in a small notebook between scenes — a return to her pre-powers private-narrative habit, which the file reads as self-soothing.

This was the Subject at her most stable in years: still over-functioning, still under-sleeping, but operating from an integrated self-concept and a recovered family rhythm. The death event interrupted exactly this convalescence.

## 2. The Death Event (*Amazing Spider-Man* #26, June 2023)

The operational facts: while assisting Peter Parker against an Orchis kill team coordinated by the operative known as Emily Bright, the Subject took a lethal strike — impalement, on Mary Jane Watson's behalf — that her morphic healing could not outrun. She died on-panel, in costume, in the presence of Peter Parker. Her body was returned to her parents in Jersey City; the *funeral* (issue #26 / surrounding tie-ins) was the first time in the canon that the Khan household was depicted in pure mourning — Muneeba publicly inconsolable, Yusuf silent and visibly aged in a single page, Aamir reading janazah, the local Muslim community filling the home in the traditional pattern of condolence visits (the three-day reception, food brought by neighbors, the women's gathering separately, the recitations).

Several diagnostic granularities from the funeral sequence and *Fallen Friend* (2023):

- **The body was washed and shrouded according to Islamic rite.** This is canonically depicted. The Subject's *first* posthumous handling was by her own community, in her own tradition — a fact she would later (post-resurrection) describe as having mattered to her in a way she had not expected.
- **The costume was retired ritually**, not bureaucratically. Bruno (returned from Wakanda for the funeral), Carol, and Aamir each kept items.
- **Carol Danvers' grief was conspicuous and unreconciled.** The Subject had never fully metabolized the *Civil War II* rupture; Carol now had to grieve someone who had not finished forgiving her. This asymmetry is load-bearing for the current relational state.
- **Peter Parker's guilt** was acute and public. The Subject's death entered Spider-Man's long catalog of "people who died adjacent to me," and his subsequent contact with her family carries the texture of penitential visitation.

## 3. The Mutant Retcon and Resurrection

Within days (Marvel-time) of the funeral, the X-Men line moved. The X-protocols revealed that the Subject's genome carried a latent X-gene that the Terrigen Mist had activated — meaning that her "Inhuman" classification had been a category error from the start, and that she qualified for Krakoan resurrection under the Five protocols. She was resurrected.

Operational specifics of the resurrection and its aftermath:

- **Continuity of memory and somatic identity was preserved**, including the death itself. The Subject remembers being killed. She remembers the funeral via post-revival briefing and via her family's account.
- **The body returned is morphologically identical** to the body that died — her polymorphic powers function as before; the X-gene reclassification did not alter phenotype, only ontology.
- **The disclosure to her family** was managed in stages. Yusuf accepted with the same gentle theological elasticity he had brought to her becoming Inhuman ("Allah's creation is wider than we are taught"). Muneeba's reaction was harder, slower, and ultimately structured by the simple fact that her daughter was alive again — affect overrode taxonomy. Aamir's response was the most theologically wrestled-with: he had read her janazah, he had buried her, and now she was at the table. He took weeks. The on-page reconciliation between Aamir and Kamala in *The New Mutant* is one of the most emotionally substantive sibling beats in her file.
- **Public disclosure of mutant status** was handled by Kamala herself, on her own timetable, with characteristic deflection of melodrama. She framed it less as a coming-out and more as a clarification.

## 4. *Ms. Marvel: The New Mutant* and Integration with the X-Line (2023–2024)

The Ahmed-scripted miniseries that followed her resurrection is the Subject's primary on-record processing of the death-and-rebirth event, and it is processed *characteristically* — i.e., obliquely, through action, with avoidance as the dominant mode.

Behavioral observations from this interval:

- **She did not seek therapy** despite the X-line's nominal availability of telepathic and conventional psychiatric resources. When pressed by Emma Frost or Jean Grey-adjacent contacts, she deflected, citing time pressure or the availability of family support. The file reads this as continuous with her pre-existing avoidance-predominant trauma signature.
- **She trained.** Beast-adjacent and Wolverine-adjacent training sequences show her drilling combat, not powers — i.e., working on the things her body cannot regenerate from rather than the things it can.
- **She integrated into the X-Men proper** as part of Jed MacKay's *X-Men* roster (vol. 6, 2024), serving on a team led by Cyclops in opposition to Orchis during the "Fall of X" endgame. This was, objectively, the most powerful institutional affiliation of her career. She handled it with her standard pattern: under-claim, do the work, build coalitions horizontally with teammates rather than seeking vertical recognition.
- **Relational granularities** within the X-roster: a quick warm working rapport with Magik (Illyana, who reads as one of the few teammates Kamala does not feel the need to translate herself for); cautious respect for Cyclops as a commander but visible discomfort with the militancy of the late-Krakoan posture; gentle, almost teacherly relationships with younger mutant children encountered on missions.
- **The Orchis confrontation** — payback, on the Subject's part, was not a primary motivator. She fought Orchis as a structural opponent (it had built the apparatus that killed her and was building worse for mutants generally) rather than as a personal nemesis. Notably, when situations brought her into proximity with Emily Bright or other operatives connected to her killing, she did not seek private vengeance. The file reads this as ego-syntonic: revenge was never in her toolkit, and the resurrection did not install it.

## 5. The Stormranger Echo and the Mutant Body

A subtle but significant thread in this period: the Subject's *relationship with her own morphic biology* has shifted. Pre-death, her power was theorized as Inhuman polymorphism; post-resurrection, the same somatic capacities are now categorized as mutant. The phenomenology is unchanged but the framing is different, and the Subject — narrative thinker that she is — has reframed accordingly.

Observable consequences:

- **She uses the powers slightly differently.** Less of the "embiggened fist" splash and more elongation, reach, body-as-tool fluency. The file reads this as a quiet integration of her body as a *practiced* instrument rather than as a contested object.
- **The Stormranger memory is dormant but not erased.** Subject does not voluntarily refer to it. When the topic of Kree tech arises adjacent to her, body-language tells: brief stillness, subject change.
- **Healing-by-reverting still applies**, which means her resurrected body still cannot maintain a disguise under stress. The original psychological reading — *a body that cannot fake itself* — remains operative and is, post-mutant-disclosure, more thematically resonant than ever.

## 6. Family State (Current)

The Khan household as of the most recent observable canon:

- **Yusuf Khan.** Aged visibly through the death event. His role as emotional anchor unchanged but his health a low-grade background concern in the file. He has expanded his theological reading in the direction of mystical and pluralist Islamic traditions — likely a private response to having a daughter who keeps changing categories. He prays for her audibly, which she has begun (per recent panels) to find comforting rather than embarrassing.
- **Muneeba Khan.** The grief-and-return cycle changed her. The controlling-anxious register that defined her pre-death has not vanished but has been displaced by something closer to *gratitude-anxiety* — a constant low-grade awareness that her daughter is a finite returned object. She hugs Kamala on arrival and departure more than she used to. She still disapproves of patrol; she stopped trying to forbid it.
- **Aamir and Tyesha.** Stable. Their child is the Subject's nearest living charge, and the role of *khala* (aunt) has become structurally important to her identity in a way the file flags as protective.
- **Bruno Carrelli.** Returned from Wakanda for the funeral and has remained in closer contact since. The hand-injury wound, the romantic non-arrival, and the death-and-resurrection asymmetry have settled into a stable friendship that is no longer being asked to be more than it is. This is an improvement.
- **The Jersey City community.** Continues to function as the Subject's outer protective ring. The Circle Q, the mosque, her old high school cohort (Nakia foremost) — these constitute a horizontal support network that the Avengers/Champions/X-Men affiliations have never replaced and that she returns to with measurable affective relief.

## 7. Current Status — Operational, Relational, Psychological

**Operational.** Active on the X-Men main roster (post-Krakoa "From the Ashes" continuity), with parallel availability to the Champions and to ad hoc Avengers/Spider-Man calls. She remains a Jersey City–based hero in residence; she has resisted relocation to any X-facility, preferring commute. She is no longer a teenager (canon-aged into late college years), and her self-presentation has subtly matured: the costume has gone through a series of competent iterations (still recognizably Wilson/Alphona-derived, less hand-stitched in execution), her speech registers carry fewer fandom-reflex tics and more dry adult cadence, though the underlying register is unchanged.

**Relational.** Carol Danvers — still complicated, now permanently asymmetric (Carol grieved her; she has not finished the *Civil War II* work; this is held in suspension). Bruno — friend, stabilized. X-Men teammates — durable working relationships, particularly with Magik and with younger team members. Spider-Man — quasi-familial affection with low-grade mutual guilt. Family — closer than ever, and structurally central. Romantic life — quiet; no current attachment of operational significance.

**Psychological.** The Subject is, by the standards of her own file, functioning well. The integrative capacity that the workup identifies as her central asset has absorbed the death-and-resurrection event and the mutant reclassification without fragmenting. She has added another category to her self-description ("Pakistani / American / Muslim / Jersey / mutant / hero / daughter / sister / aunt / writer") and held it. The unprocessed material remains: she has not narrated her own death, has not therapeutically engaged it, and avoids the topic with the polite firmness she uses for all topics she has decided not to discuss. The file's prediction is that this material will surface event-bound rather than spontaneously — likely triggered by a future threat to a family member, a future moral injury from an authority figure, or proximity to her own death-circumstances (Orchis-residue, Bright-adjacent encounters).

**Risk profile, current.** Self-directed risk: moderate-elevated, via the unchanged over-functioning and chronic sleep deprivation, now compounded by an unprocessed mortality experience and an organizational affiliation (X-Men) that runs higher casualty rates than her prior teams. Other-directed risk: negligible; she has not become more violent post-resurrection, has not adopted any of the harder-edged X-line operational postures, and continues to refuse predictive or pre-emptive force. Corruption risk: still near-zero, for the reasons identified in the synthesized read — her identity is plural by practice and cannot be split by appeals to any one of its parts; the addition of the mutant axis has, if anything, reinforced this.

**Where she is, right now.** Jersey City. Probably at her parents' kitchen table, or on a fire escape with a notebook, or on a rooftop somewhere between the waterfront and the Circle Q, or in transit to an X-mission she will not tell her mother the details of, or babysitting her niece. She is twenty, give or take canon's elasticity. She has died once and come back. She is still the moral spine of any room she enters, and she still doesn't quite believe she is.


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 03: MEDICAL HISTORY

## Subject: Kamala Khan (Khan, Kamala; b. Jersey City, NJ; South Asian/Pakistani descent, maternal lineage Karachi)

---

## 3.1 Constitutional Baseline & Pre-Exposure Somatic Record

Pre-Terrigenesis, the subject presents as an unremarkable adolescent female of Punjabi-Pakistani descent: olive-toned skin (Fitzpatrick III), dark brown eyes, dark brown hair worn at shoulder length, height approximately 5'3" at age sixteen, weight in the 105–115 lb range, normative BMI for ethnicity and age. Right-hand dominant. No reported congenital anomalies, no childhood hospitalizations of note. Standard New Jersey pediatric vaccination schedule inferred from her enrollment at Coles Academic High School (mandatory MMR, Tdap, varicella, HPV-eligible cohort).

Dental: visibly intact, mild posterior crowding consistent with un-orthodonticized middle-class American adolescence; no braces depicted at any point in the record. Ocular: no corrective lenses, no documented refractive error. Audition: intact, with above-baseline auditory attention to ambient cultural cues (a behavioral observation, not a pathology).

**Pre-existing somatic patterns of note:**

- **Episodic tension headaches**, inferable from sustained school/family/secret-life triple-loading; she is depicted clutching her temples, pressing the bridge of her nose, and rubbing the occipital region throughout the Wilson run. Likely tension-type, possibly with a cervicogenic component from extended laptop/phone posture (fan-fic composition, AvengerCon planning).
- **Mild menstrual presence** — never depicted explicitly, but inferable: she is a sixteen-year-old female across multi-year canon and has never been shown with the gynecologic complications that would mark her as anything but normative.
- **No documented allergies**. The bacon-aversion is religious-cultural, not IgE-mediated.

---

## 3.2 The Master Medical Event: Terrigenesis (Inhumanity #1 / Ms. Marvel vol. 3 #1)

Walking home from the waterfront pier party along the Jersey City riverfront, the subject is enveloped by the Terrigen Mist released during the dispersal arc that triggered global Inhuman/now-mutant manifestations. Mechanism: airborne mutagenic crystalline particulate, inhaled and dermally absorbed, initiating cellular reorganization in latent X-positive substrates (subsequently retconned in *Fallen Friend* and *X-Men* (2024) — the Terrigen acted as an environmental activator of a previously-silent mutant phenotype rather than as the source of Inhuman heritage).

**Cocooning phase:** Approximately several hours of full-body chrysalis enclosure. Subject reports auditory and visual hallucinosis during enclosure — appearance of Captain Marvel, Iron Man, and Captain America reciting Urdu poetry (Amir Khusrau's "Aaj Rang Hai"), which is diagnostically significant as the first overt manifestation of the integrative-via-syncretism identity work that will become her dominant adaptive pattern. The hallucination is benign, ego-syntonic, lucid in retrospect — not psychotic, not a marker of any subsequent vulnerability.

**Emergence presentation:** Subject extrudes from the cocoon in a morphologically reorganized body that is *not* her own: white skin, blonde hair, taller (estimated 5'9"–5'11"), in Carol Danvers' classic black/red/gold costume. This is the unconscious-wish manifestation — her novel polymorphism, presented in its earliest hours, defaulted to the form of her idealized object. *Medically* this is the most important single fact in her record: her power expresses pre-conscious affect. She will spend years learning to bring it under volitional governance, and the suppression of involuntary morphing is itself an ongoing somatic discipline analogous to learning continence.

---

## 3.3 The Polymorphic Phenotype — Operational Specifications

The acquired phenotype, persistent across Inhuman and post-retcon mutant framings, comprises:

- **Embiggening:** voluntary expansion of total cellular volume. Documented maxima: torso-on-Manhattan-rooftop scale (~25–30 feet); discrete-limb expansion to ~15 feet (her signature "giant fist" — most frequently the right, consistent with handedness). Mass apparently scales with volume in some depictions and is suspiciously absent in others (she does not crater rooftops she ought to crater); this is an under-specified canonical inconsistency that almost certainly reflects unconscious volitional control of mass-distribution, not violation of physics.
- **Shrinking ("disembiggening"):** documented to approximately doll-scale (~6 inches), used for infiltration, hiding, evasion. She uses this less than embiggening, a behavioral tell discussed in §3.7.
- **Elongation:** the predominant in-combat morph. Limbs and neck stretch to 20+ feet without volume change. Lower metabolic cost than embiggening.
- **Shape-mimicry:** limited and unreliable. She can approximate the *silhouette* of another person but not facial fidelity. The early Carol-morph was an outlier driven by unconscious wish-fulfillment; volitional impersonation has never reached that fidelity again. *This is itself medically significant — her body resists deception under conscious control.*
- **Healing-while-shifting:** the most clinically important property. Injuries are not healed by stasis; they are healed by *reverting to baseline form*. Operationally: cuts, fractures, even severe internal trauma resolve at accelerated rates *if and only if* she returns to her natal phenotype (5'3", her actual face). **Disguise and recovery are mutually exclusive.** A body that cannot hide while healing is, by design, a body that must be visible to be whole.
- **Polymorphic exhaustion:** sustained morphing depletes her — she is repeatedly shown ravenous after extended combat (gyro-binges at Circle Q and at Bruno's father's shop), and dehydrated. Caloric and water expenditure scale with shift magnitude and duration.

**Failure modes:** Under acute pain, severe sleep deprivation, or profound emotional dysregulation, she loses morph control — limbs spontaneously stretch, fists involuntarily embiggen, or, conversely, she cannot hold an enlarged form when she needs to. The Stormranger arc (see §3.5) externalizes this failure into a separable agent.

---

## 3.4 Injury Ledger (Chronological, Selected)

**Year 1 (Wilson vol. 3 #1–#19):**
- Multiple gunshot wounds (Inventor arc, Doyle robotics), low caliber, treated by morph-reset. No retained foreign bodies.
- Concussion, mild–moderate, in Inventor's lair; transient nausea, photophobia. Untreated medically; resolved by morph-reset and a nap on Bruno's couch.
- Lacerations, hands and forearms, from chrysalis emergence and from her first costume's improvised construction (sewn from a repurposed dishdasha/burkini, the needle injuries are visible if you look). Healed without scarring.
- Chronic *muscular strain* — neck, lumbar, deltoid girdle — from learning embiggening without proprioceptive training. The first six months of her career are biomechanically equivalent to a teenager who has suddenly grown six feet overnight at variable intervals.

**Years 2–3 (Last Days / Secret Wars / post-incursion):**
- Crush injuries during the incursion catastrophe; survived via shrink-evasion.
- Smoke inhalation, Jersey City fires; mild upper-airway irritation, self-limited.
- Sleep debt accumulating measurably. By the end of Year 2 her circadian disruption is severe enough that her mother begins commenting (Muneeba's "you look like a ghost" line is the canonical marker).

**Civil War II (Year 3):**
- Multiple blunt-force traumas during the predictive-arrest sweeps.
- *Witnessing trauma*: Bruno Carrelli sustains catastrophic crush injury to the left hand and forearm during the prison breakout she enabled. Bruno loses functional use of the hand; later receives a prosthetic developed in Wakanda. **This is the single most psychologically loaded medical event in her file that did not happen to her own body**, and her somatic response to it — reduced appetite, sleep onset insomnia, a several-week period of avoiding her own reflection — is itself a recognizable acute stress presentation.
- Geographic flight to Karachi (~3–6 weeks). Notable: during this interval, no costumed activity, no injuries, and she sleeps. This is the only sustained physiological recovery window in her career.

**Champions / Ahmed era (Years 4–5):**
- Stormranger-mediated injuries (see §3.5).
- Repeated kinetic trauma in team operations; standard for the role.
- A documented near-drowning during a Champions deployment; cold-water exposure, transient hypothermia.

**Outlawed (Year 5):**
- Critical injury at the Coles High Halloween event — internal hemorrhage, multi-organ insult, cardiac instability. Hospitalized; secret identity revealed in the process to her parents (a *psychological* injury concurrent with the somatic one). Recovery measured in weeks not days; her morph-reset healing is insufficient when injuries exceed a threshold her physiology cannot self-correct.
- Surgical interventions during this hospitalization are inferable but not detailed; surgical scarring noted in subsequent issues briefly.
- Psychological sequelae: the only depicted instance of her displaying frank fear of her own powers. She avoids morphing for a period post-discharge.

**Resurrection era (Year 7+):**
- **Cause of death, Amazing Spider-Man #26 (2023):** impalement, penetrating trauma to torso by Emily Bright's Orchis-issued weapon. Cardiac and great-vessel involvement. Exsanguination. Death pronounced.
- **Funeral and body disposition:** *Fallen Friend* documents the Khan family rites — ghusl performed (per her mother's insistence, Islamic burial preparation), though the body is subsequently retrieved by X-Force operatives for the resurrection protocol. The interruption of janazah is itself a wound in her mother's record that bleeds into Kamala's own.
- **Resurrection mechanism:** Krakoan/mutant protocol — Five-derived gestalt resurrection, body grown in egg, Cerebro-archived consciousness instantiated. Full somatic continuity *claimed*; somatic discontinuity *experienced*. She has, in the strict medical sense, a new body, and she knows it. She has not publicly processed this.
- Post-resurrection: full physiological function restored. Morph control intact. Re-presented as mutant rather than Inhuman; phenotype unchanged but lineage reframed.

---

## 3.5 The Stormranger Episode (Ahmed run, 2019–2020) — Detailed

A Kree biotechnological exosuit, gifted via her newly-discovered Kree paternal-line heritage, bonds to her cutaneously and behaves as a semi-autonomous nanotech symbiote. Diagnostically: it activates during her REM sleep and conducts violent operations she does not consciously authorize.

This is medically a *parasomnia with externalized agency* — the closest analogues in the human record are severe REM-behavior disorder cases, but here the behavior is purposive and remote rather than enacted in bed. The suit nearly kills her brother Aamir. She destroys it, with considerable difficulty and not without grief — the suit was, after all, doing what some part of her wanted done.

**Sequelae:** transient insomnia (fear of sleep); subsequent re-establishment of sleep, but with a permanent low-grade vigilance about her own dissociated aggressive content. She is, post-Stormranger, more honest about her anger.

---

## 3.6 Substances, Diet, Sleep, Sexuality, Menses

**Substances:** Lifetime abstinence from alcohol; the waterfront-pier refusal is the documented baseline and has held. No tobacco. No cannabis. No prescription misuse. Caffeine: chai (frequent, family-mediated, ritualized); coffee (rarely, situational). No documented use of stimulants for academic performance despite obvious motivation pressures — a notable and consistent abstention.

**Diet:** Halal-observant with effort and intermittent transgression-curiosity (the BLT scene; recurring fascination with bacon, which she does not eat). Meals are erratic — skipped during operations, binged afterward. Primary food vectors: home (Muneeba's cooking, structurally regular and emotionally weighted); Circle Q (convenience-store carbohydrates, ironic given that the same store is the scene of her foundational humiliation); Bruno's father's gyro shop (her *de facto* mess hall). Caloric intake almost certainly inadequate for her metabolic load when active, which compounds her sleep debt and contributes to her irritability under operational stress.

**Sleep:** Chronically truncated. Estimated 4–6 hours/night across the Wilson run during active periods, recovering to age-normative 8–9 only during the Karachi interval and during illness. Her bedroom (third floor of the Khan house, Marbella Drive area, Jersey City) is depicted with a perpetually unmade bed and a desk-light habitually on — a behavioral marker of disrupted onset.

**Sexuality:** Heteronormative orientation inferable; sexual activity essentially absent from the record. Romantic interest is depicted (Bruno; later, Red Dagger/Kareem) but physical expression is limited to embraces and one or two chaste kisses. This is consistent with a religiously observant adolescent and is *not* a marker of inhibition pathology.

**Menses:** Normative by inference; no depicted dysmenorrhea, no PMDD features.

---

## 3.7 The Body as Tell — Behavioral Somatics

A body that cannot be disguised while healing is a body whose damage cannot be hidden from her mother. This single physiological fact organizes much of her domestic deception architecture: she returns home morph-reset and intact precisely *because* her physiology demands it, which means Muneeba sees a daughter without bruises and is gaslit by the subject's own biology. Yusuf, who looks more carefully, sees the exhaustion that does not heal — the shadowed eyes, the slowed gait, the appetite suppression.

**Embiggening vs. shrinking ratio:** approximately 8:1 across the canon. She uses bigness an order of magnitude more often than smallness. This is the medical/somatic correlate of her psychological adaptation: she has decided, at the level of practiced movement, to take up space rather than to disappear. The Carol-morph emergence was the temptation to disappear into someone else; the giant fist is the corrective.

**Right-fist dominance in embiggening:** the right hand is enlarged in combat more than 70% of depicted instances, consistent with handedness, but also consistent with the affective valence of the gesture (the punch-as-assertion vs. the open-hand-as-supplication, which she does *not* embiggen).

**Reversion-tic:** when she demorphs to baseline she frequently rubs her own face, as if confirming it is hers. This is a micro-ritual of identity-reclamation. It begins after the Carol-emergence and never leaves her.

**Stress-somatics:** under acute stress she displays — in order of escalation — (1) jaw clench and rapid blink, (2) involuntary fist embiggening (often suppressed back down within a second), (3) elongation of the dominant arm without intent, (4) loss of containment in the lower limbs (a "noodling" of stance her enemies have not yet learned to read), (5) reversion-collapse, in which she involuntarily snaps to baseline and cannot remorph for several minutes — a physiological circuit-breaker.

---

## 3.8 Iatrogenic and Identity-Reframing Events

Three retconnings of her ontological category have occurred within her medical record: Inhuman (origin), mutant (post-Krakoa), and the unresolved interaction with Kree heritage during the Stormranger interval. Each reframing is *medically real* to her in the sense that it changes her sense of what her body is and to whom it belongs. The mutant reframing, in particular, places her in a third stigmatized community concurrent with the first two (Pakistani-American, Muslim). Her response — acceptance with grace — is consistent with the integrative capacity established in §3 of the master workup, but the somatic cost has not been documented and is likely under-reported by the subject herself, who is constitutionally averse to claiming wounds.

---

## 3.9 Unresolved Medical Issues, Open File

1. **Post-resurrection somatic continuity.** Subjectively she is herself. Objectively, the body is regrown. She has not sought, and the narrative has not provided, any acknowledgment of the discontinuity. This is the single largest gap in her self-care record.
2. **Cumulative sleep debt.** Chronic, never repaid except during withdrawal episodes. Long-term cognitive and immunologic consequences are deferred but not abolished.
3. **Mass-conservation paradox.** Her embiggening physics are not fully consistent with classical mass conservation. Whatever pocket-dimensional or quantum reservoir is supplying the mass is uncatalogued, and the long-term consequences of repeatedly drawing on it are unknown to her and to her physicians (she does not have physicians).
4. **Bruno's hand as somatic referent.** She does not have the injury; she carries it. Her right wrist is, on at least three documented occasions, unconsciously cradled by her left hand during conversations about him. This is not her wound, but it is on her body.
5. **The interrupted ghusl.** Her mother performed Islamic burial preparation on her body, which was then taken and regrown. There is no protocol — religious, medical, or psychological — for what that means. It is an open file in every sense.

---

*End Section 03. Cross-reference Section 04 (Psychiatric) for sequelae of the events catalogued here; Section 07 (Domestic/Routine) for the daily management of the polymorphic body within the Khan household.*


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS: KAMALA KHAN

*A longitudinal mapping of the body as it actually moves through a day, a week, a crisis, a decade. Compiled from continuous observational record (Jersey City, Karachi, Manhattan, Krakoa, and points between); cross-referenced against pre- and post-Terrigenesis baselines.*

---

## 1. BASELINE MORPHOLOGY AND THE PROBLEM OF "BASELINE"

The first analytic difficulty in any somatic file on Subject is that she has, since age sixteen, possessed no single resting body. Pre-Terrigenesis baseline: 5'3", approximately 115 lb, South Asian, brown-black hair worn mid-back length and usually braided, brown eyes, a small scar above the right eyebrow (childhood — cricket bat, brother Aamir, ages 9 and 11 respectively), no piercings until late adolescence (a single pair, lobes, sterling studs at her mother's insistence for a cousin's wedding), no tattoos at any point (religious prohibition; she has discussed considering henna and stops there).

Post-Terrigenesis, her *true* form remains exactly this — and this is itself a forensic detail. Injury reverts her. Exhaustion reverts her. Sleep reverts her. The body that emerges when she is too tired or too hurt to perform anything else is the body she was born with, and the morphic field she generates is, in operational terms, a costume her cells wear at her will. The file therefore distinguishes between **baseline body**, **operational morphology** (size-shifted, elongated, embiggened), and **transitional state** (mid-shift, partial, leaking — usually under stress).

Skin tone: warm medium brown, slightly olive undertone, sun-responsive — summers in Jersey deepen her to roughly two shades darker than her January color, and a documented behavioral tell is that she stops noticing this until her mother comments. Hair: thick, with a natural wave that surfaces in humidity and is otherwise straightened by daily braiding; she sheds visibly into her hairbrush and pillowcase, and the loss pattern is normal for her age, no thinning. Hands: small, square palms, blunt fingertips, nails kept short and unpainted (she has tried polish three documented times in canon, each removed within forty-eight hours, citing "it gets weird when I embiggen"). Right index and middle fingers bear a permanent faint indentation from pen-grip — she writes by hand more than her cohort, the residue of fan-fiction notebooks. Left wrist: a thin pale stretch-mark band, post-Terrigenesis, from an early elongation attempt held too long.

## 2. FACE: THE WORKING SURFACE

Her face is the most legible part of her, and she knows it, and she has not learned to control it. This is significant: a girl who can rearrange her cellular volume cannot reliably keep her own eyebrows from telegraphing what she thinks of you.

**Eyes.** Brown, large relative to face, with a documented tendency toward what observers consistently describe as "wide" — her resting state is mild ocular openness, which reads as alertness and which she leverages, semi-consciously, to appear younger and less threatening than she is. Blink rate: elevated above population mean during conversation with authority figures (Carol Danvers, Tony Stark, her mother in disciplinary mode), suppressed below mean during sustained focus (combat assessment, reading, writing). Sclera reddens after long patrols; she rubs the inner canthi with her knuckle, not her fingertip, a self-soothing tic inherited from her father.

**Eyebrows.** Thick, expressive, the single most reliable readout. Calm: relaxed, slight natural arch. Concentrated: drawn together, vertical crease at glabella. Surprised (a common state): launched upward in synchrony. Skeptical: left brow lifts independently, right stays — this is asymmetric and stable across years; it is her tell when she is being polite about something she does not believe. She does not know she does this.

**Mouth.** Small, mobile. Resting mouth is slightly parted, not pursed — another youth-coding feature. Smiles run wide and fast, frequently with a small dimple in the left cheek only. She bites her lower lip when thinking and the inside of her right cheek when stressed; the latter has produced a chronic small ulceration that flares during exam weeks, *Civil War II*, and the *Outlawed* arc. When she lies (rarely, badly) she presses her lips together and looks down-left.

**Nose.** Wrinkles when she laughs hard. Crinkles in disgust (the BLT scene). Flares slightly during combat exertion.

**Jaw.** Soft baseline. Clenched in her sleep — confirmed by the *Stormranger* arc and prior, with morning soreness she ascribes to "weird dreams." Her father has the same nocturnal bruxism.

**Microexpressions of note.**
- Pre-suppression of a grin: lower lip rolls inward briefly before she successfully neutralizes her face. Occurs in classrooms, in mosque, in briefings.
- Pre-suppression of tears: chin dimples, throat works once, then she laughs.
- Anger onset: a half-second stillness across the whole face — total cessation of her usual microactivity — before her brows come down. This is the moment opponents who have studied her should fear; it precedes either an embiggened fist or a sentence she will not retract.

## 3. POSTURE, GAIT, AND SPATIAL HABIT

**Standing.** Default posture is slightly forward-shouldered, a residue of years of slouching at lockers, over laptops, over notebooks. Her mother has corrected this posture across two decades of canon; it briefly improves and reverts within hours. She stands with her weight on her right leg, left leg slightly bent, a contrapposto that gives her a perpetual look of being about to leave the room.

**Sitting.** Cross-legged whenever permitted — on chairs, on beds, on rooftops, on the floor. In formal settings (briefings, school) she sits with knees together, feet hooked behind the chair leg, hands in her lap, fingers worrying each other. At home she sits on the kitchen counter when Muneeba is not looking. On rooftops (her single most documented location) she sits with knees drawn up, arms wrapped around shins, chin on knees — a self-enclosing posture that is also her preferred thinking position.

**Gait.** Quick, slightly bouncing, toes pointed faintly inward (mild physiological in-toeing, not corrected). Step length shorter than her stride would allow — she walks small, again a youth- and femininity-coded compression that she does not deploy strategically so much as default into. In combat or pursuit, the gait opens completely: she runs with a long lope, surprising in someone who walks like she does.

**As size-shifted body.** When embiggened to two to three times normal, her gait grows heavier and her step deliberate, and she develops a noticeable lean forward at the hips — she has not fully solved her own biomechanics at scale, and the file notes she fights better at moderate increase (50–100%) than at maximum. At minimum size (small enough to fit in a fist) she moves like a startled bird, twitchy, head-cocking, unsuited to it; she dislikes shrinking and does it rarely.

**Spatial habits.** She gravitates to walls and corners in unfamiliar rooms, sits with her back to the wall in restaurants, and chooses the seat with the best sightline to the door in any briefing. None of this is trained; all of it is the unconscious geometry of a girl who has been the object of hostile attention in public spaces since elementary school. She does not perceive herself as doing it.

She touches surfaces as she passes them — fingertips trailing along lockers, banisters, the edge of a kitchen counter. In Bruno's family's deli, she touches the same corner of the same display case every entry, a ritual that long predates the period of her grief over him.

## 4. HANDS, GESTURE, AND THE VOCABULARY OF MOTION

Her hands are in constant low-amplitude motion. When she speaks she gestures with both hands forward, palms slightly up, fingers spread — the gesture vocabulary of explanation and pleading rather than declaration. She rarely points; when she does, it is with the whole hand, not a finger.

**Tics and self-touch.**
- Right thumb rubs across the pads of right index and middle fingers when thinking — a soft, repetitive friction, audible at close range.
- Tucks hair behind her left ear (only the left) approximately every three to five minutes when it is loose, regardless of whether hair is actually displaced.
- Adjusts her scarf or hijab (worn variably and contextually — to mosque always, to school never, around family elders often) by gripping the front center fold and tugging downward once.
- When seated, traces patterns on her own kneecap with a fingernail — usually letters, sometimes the shapes of lightning bolts and stars from her sketchbooks.
- Cracks the knuckles of her right hand only, by pressing the fingers backward against her left palm, when bored.

**Writing/drawing posture.** Left-handed for fine motor (drawing, doodling), right-handed for utility (writing, eating, throwing). This functional ambidexterity is unusual and unremarked in canon; it manifests in her sketchbooks, which she fills with right-side-of-page text and left-side-of-page drawings, an organization that is invisible to her and consistent across years.

**In combat.** Hands open more than closed — she throws with embiggened palms, catches, swats, blocks. Fist-fighting is a secondary mode; she prefers a giant open hand to a giant fist. This is psychologically coherent: she is a stopper, not a striker. She has never, on record, thrown a punch at a face she could have caught instead.

## 5. VOCAL PROFILE AND BREATH

Mid-to-upper register, mild Jersey vowels (the *a* in "Avengers" foregrounds her geography), code-switches downward in pitch and slows in cadence when speaking to her parents, particularly her mother in Urdu — and upward, faster, in higher peer registers especially online and around fellow nerds. She uses internet-native syntax in speech ("I literally cannot," "no but actually"), runs sentences together when excited, and develops a slight stammer at moments of moral conflict — not at moments of fear. Fear focuses her speech; ethics fragment it.

**Laughter.** Loud, surprised-sounding, often louder than she intends, frequently followed by a hand over the mouth — a reflex acquired from her mother's chronic shushing in public. The hand-clap is rare but signature in moments of delight; she will clap once, sharply, when delighted by an idea, then immediately look embarrassed.

**Breath.** Diaphragmatic at rest, shallow under stress. She holds her breath while reading something difficult — both her father and Bruno have, at separate points across the canon, told her to breathe. She forgets and re-forgets. In combat her breath is audible and rhythmic; in moral confrontation it goes silent and then resumes in a single sigh.

## 6. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

Chronically disrupted across the entire post-power record. Pre-power baseline was already sub-optimal (late-night writing, fan forums until 2 a.m., chronic morning resistance). Post-power, sleep onset is delayed (patrols, homework displaced into nighttime), sleep maintenance is poor (calls, alerts, ambient guilt), and total time-in-bed averages 5.5–6.5 hours by inference across her schedules.

**Position.** Side-sleeper, curled, left side preferred, left hand under cheek. Right knee drawn up higher than left. Pulls covers to chin. Often falls asleep on top of an open laptop or a book; the file has noted her waking with a textbook imprint on her cheek on multiple documented mornings.

**Parasomnias.** Bruxism (jaw clenching). Sleep-talking, sporadic, mostly single words or names ("Carol," "Bruno," "Abu") that she does not remember. During the *Stormranger* period: episodic somnambulism with violent behavior, exogenously driven by the Kree suit but indicative of a baseline susceptibility to dissociated motor activity under load. Post-resurrection: documented difficulty distinguishing sleep onset from "the dark place," a private phrase she has used to no one but has written once in a margin.

**Wake pattern.** Slow, multiple alarm dismissals, reliant on Muneeba's escalating calls from the hallway. Reaches for phone before opening both eyes. First conscious motion: rubbing the right eye with the right knuckle (the same gesture she uses for tired sclera mid-day).

## 7. EATING

Disordered in pattern, not in pathology. Skipped breakfasts, large irregular dinners when she remembers, snacks driven by emotional state and convenience: chai with two sugars at home, gyros from Mr. Carrelli's shop after school or after patrol, samosas at family gatherings consumed standing, gas-station candy on rooftops at 2 a.m.

**Halal observance** is sincere and effortful. She does not eat pork; the smell of bacon evokes documented ambivalence (curiosity, then guilt, then re-affirmation). She has been observed sniffing pork products approximately four times across canon and consumed none. Alcohol: zero, lifetime. Caffeine: rising across her teen years, chai then drip coffee then, by Champions era, an espresso-shop habit she conceals from her parents.

**Eating posture.** Fast, head-down, often standing or walking. At family table she slows, eats with her right hand, often with bread (roti, naan) rather than utensil for curry, in line with household practice. With non-family she becomes self-conscious about eating and either eats less or jokes more, depending on company.

**Ramadan.** Observed seriously; she patrols less, sleeps differently, and her morale-cognition decouples — physically lower energy, spiritually elevated mood, a documented annual cycle since age fourteen.

## 8. GROOMING AND DRESS

**Hair.** Washed every other day, oiled weekly (a maternal practice she has internalized), braided for sleep, single braid or low ponytail for school, loose for special occasions. She brushes hair while thinking; the brush is a thinking-object.

**Skin.** She has been treated for adolescent acne; residual is mild and concentrated at the chin. She picks at it under stress — a thumbnail-and-index pinch that her mother has slapped her hand away from since childhood. Moisturizer is inconsistent, sunscreen is nonexistent, and the file notes that her father is the only person who has successfully gotten her to wear it (a single tube of SPF 30 on her dresser, half-used over three years).

**Dress.** Layered, modest by personal choice rather than strict prescription, oriented toward comfort and color. Long-sleeved tees over long-sleeved tees, cardigans, scarves, jeans, sneakers (Converse and similar, scuffed). T-shirts feature graphics — bands, slogans, fandoms — that she chooses semi-strategically as conversation-starters with potential allies and that she does not realize function as identification badges. Costume is hand-modified, repurposed dishdasha base, lightning-bolt motif, scarf as cowl; she repairs it herself, and the stitching evolves visibly across years from amateur to competent.

**Jewelry.** Minimal. Stud earrings, intermittent. A thin gold chain (gift from her grandmother, religious) worn under clothing, untouched in public, fingered at the collarbone in moments of acute stress — a private gesture, not visible to most.

## 9. SEXUAL AND ROMANTIC SOMATICS

Muted, conflicted, and contoured by both religious commitment and personal wariness. The somatic record is necessarily thin: she has not been documented in sexual activity. Romantic touch with Bruno across years is hand-brushing, shoulder-leaning, the long hug that holds three beats past the platonic threshold and is then broken by one of them — usually her — with a joke. Her body when in proximity to Bruno is noticeably stiller than her usual baseline: gesture-rate drops, breath shallows, the thumb-pad friction tic accelerates. With other romantic interests across the canon, the pattern is similar: bodily quieting, then over-verbalization to fill the silence the body left.

**Physical affection in non-romantic contexts** is high. She hugs her father openly, her mother in negotiated moments, her brother under protest from both, Bruno freely until the post-injury period and tentatively after. She is a hugger in greeting and goodbye and an arm-link walker with female friends. Touch with mentors (Carol, especially) is restrained — she does not initiate, and when Carol initiates she goes still in a way that reads as reverence and is also self-protection.

## 10. STATE-DEPENDENT VARIATION

**Calm.** Forward-shouldered, expressive face, hand-talker, audible breath, frequent self-touch (hair, knee, finger pads), high baseline motion, easy laughter.

**Concentrated.** Stillness in the body, mouth slightly open, eyes narrowed, blink suppressed, one hand at the chin or worrying the lower lip, the other tracing patterns on a surface. Breath held in long phases.

**Excited (fan / nerd / discovery).** Whole-body engagement: bouncing on balls of feet, hands flapping briefly at chest height before she remembers herself, the single sharp clap, voice up half an octave, words tumbling. The body she would have if no one were watching.

**Embarrassed.** Shoulders inward, hand to back of neck, eyes down-left, an audible exhaled laugh that is more sigh than laugh, a stepping-backward of half a pace.

**Stressed (low-grade, chronic).** Cheek-biting (right side), nail-tracing on kneecap, hair-tucking accelerating to once a minute, posture compressing further, eating-rate increasing or food-skipping deepening — both extremes present in record.

**Morally injured.** This is her most distinctive state. The body goes quiet. Gestures cease. The face holds the half-second pre-anger stillness and then does not resolve into anger; it resolves into a kind of withdrawal. Eye contact with the offender is maintained too long. Voice drops in volume and steadies. She has been observed in this state during her final confrontations with Carol in *Civil War II* and during the public framing of Kamala's Law. It is the state in which she is most dangerous to herself, because the next step from it is geographic flight or somatic over-extension.

**Threat (acute combat).** Gait opens, breath becomes audible-rhythmic, hands open and forward, eyes track in saccades across the field, mouth often slightly open. Verbalization continues — she quips through combat, both as nerve-management and as outward signal of non-lethal intent. When the threat escalates past her own margin of safety, the quipping stops, and the silence is the marker.

**Intimacy (familial / close friendship).** Posture drops fully — she leans, she sprawls, she lays her head on her father's shoulder, she sits on the floor at her mother's feet during television. Gesture amplitude shrinks; speech slows; the code-switch downward in pitch is most pronounced. The body that emerges in her family kitchen is, demonstrably, the body she most wants to inhabit.

**Post-trauma (the avoidance-predominant signature).** Hyper-normality. Increased humor output, increased social availability, decreased solitude, increased volume. The body works overtime to perform that nothing has happened, and the cost shows in the disrupted sleep, the deepened cheek ulceration, the chain-fingering that she does not know she is doing.

---

## 11. AGGREGATE READ

The body of Subject is, like the rest of her, organized around a tension between visibility and invisibility — and like the rest of her, it has been resolving that tension toward a difficult, hard-won integration. Her face shows what she feels, and she has stopped trying to stop it. Her gait is small, but it opens when she runs. Her hands are restless because they have not yet been given enough to hold. She sleeps badly because the world wakes her, and she eats badly because she is feeding too many selves at once, and she touches her grandmother's chain when she is afraid because the body remembers what the mind is busy denying.

Operationally: she is identifiable at distance by the bounce in her step and the angle of her shoulders; at middle range by the eyebrow asymmetry and the hair-tuck; at close range by the pad-of-thumb friction and the held breath. The pre-anger stillness is the single most useful predictive marker in her file. Any analyst, ally, or adversary who learns to read it has approximately half a second to choose what happens next.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 6: ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## 6.1 The Etiological Architecture: A Secure Home Inside a Hostile Perimeter

The single most analytically important fact about Kamala Khan's attachment system is its inversion of the modal Western superhero etiology. She is not an orphan. She is not estranged. She did not flee. The Khan house at 226 Marigold Lane, Jersey City, is — across nearly a decade of canon — depicted as functionally warm: shared meals occur with regularity (the family dinner is a recurring panel-furniture across the Wilson and Ahmed runs), parental presence is constant, the father is physically affectionate (hand on shoulder, top-of-head kiss, the recurring "*beta*"), and the mother's anxiety is consistently legible to all parties as love-expressed-as-control rather than as withholding. There is no abuse, no abandonment, no alcoholic parent, no parentified-child structure preceding the powers.

What this produces, in attachment terms, is a child with a **predominantly secure internal working model of intimate others** layered beneath an **insecure-vigilant working model of the social macro-environment**. Love is reliable; the *world* is the problem. This split is the master key to every relational pattern she displays as Ms. Marvel.

The granularity matters. With Yusuf she demonstrates classic secure-base behaviors: she returns to him after rupture (the late-Wilson scene where he reveals he knows about her powers, and her relief is so complete she folds into him without speech); she uses him as a referent during moral uncertainty ("what would Abu say?" surfaces as a private check at least a dozen times across the canon); and she tolerates his disapproval without catastrophizing it, because she has never had to. With Muneeba the pattern is **ambivalent-resistant but durable** — Kamala lies, evades, sneaks out, gets caught, weeps, is forgiven, lies again. The cycle does not erode the bond because both parties tacitly understand the lying is about preserving Muneeba from a truth that would hurt her (the costume, the danger), not about contempt for her. When Kamala finally tells her mother everything (Wilson, late run), Muneeba's response — "I always knew you were special, I just didn't know how" — is the moment that retroactively converts the ambivalent pattern into a secure one. Few superheroes get that conversation. It is structurally load-bearing.

With Aamir, the sibling bond is **secure with rivalrous coloration** — early canon plays him as the over-devout, under-employed older brother she gently mocks; later canon (his marriage to Tyesha, his abduction during the Ahmed run, the Stormranger nearly killing him) reveals an almost ferocious protective register beneath the sibling banter. Note the somatic tell: when Aamir is threatened, Kamala does not embiggen; she **shrinks and runs to him**, which is the attachment behavior of a younger sibling, not a hero. Body remembers role.

## 6.2 The Generalization: How a Securely-Attached Child Behaves in Public

The standard prediction for a child with this profile is high relational competence, broad coalition-building, low suspicion at first contact, durable friendships, and difficulty with the specific subclass of betrayals that come from idealized authority figures. Kamala displays all five with textbook fidelity.

**Broad coalition.** Her social graph in Jersey City is anomalously wide for a teenage hero. Bruno Carrelli (childhood); Nakia Bahadir (mosque, school); Mike (Bruno's later girlfriend, whom Kamala befriends rather than freezes out); Zoe Zimmer (initial bully, eventual close friend and out lesbian whose coming-out Kamala receives without flinching); Josh (the boyfriend-of-bully who becomes a victim she fails to protect); Gabe (Doc.X arc); the Champions roster (Viv, Sam, Miles, Amadeus, Riri); the Red Dagger (Kareem); her mosque community; Sheikh Abdullah; her neighborhood at large, which physically turns out *en masse* in two separate storylines to defend her. This is not a hero with three friends and a sidekick. This is a hero embedded in a *parish*.

**Low initial suspicion.** Her default greeting posture across the canon — observed in panel after panel — is open hands, slight forward lean, raised eyebrows, half-smile. She makes eye contact early and holds it. She introduces herself by first name without rank. New team members are integrated within an issue or two; she does not haze, test, or vet. This is the body language of a child who has not been taught that strangers are dangerous in the small-scale sense — only the structural sense.

**Difficulty with idealized-authority betrayal.** This is the diagnostic seam, addressed in detail below.

## 6.3 The Carol Danvers Template: Idealization, Devotion, Rupture, Slow Repair

The Kamala–Carol relationship is the most psychologically dense in the canon and must be read attachment-theoretically, not merely as mentorship.

**Phase 1 — Pre-contact idealization (pre-2014 through *Ms. Marvel* #1).** Kamala loved Carol Danvers before she met her. The Avengers fan-fic, the bedroom poster, the inhalation of Carol's lore — these are the markers of a **parasocial primary attachment** to an imagined caregiver. The literal manifestation of Carol's body when Kamala first uses her powers is the most extreme externalization of an idealized-object attachment in modern superhero literature: she does not merely want to be like Carol, her body briefly *becomes* Carol. Attachment in adolescence is supposed to migrate from parents to peers and romantic partners; Kamala's migrated to an icon.

**Phase 2 — First contact and graceful incorporation (Wilson run, mid-arc).** When Carol actually appears, the dynamic is generous. Carol does the correct thing — acknowledges the legacy gift of the name, offers tactical advice, treats Kamala as a peer-in-training rather than a fan. Kamala's behavioral tells in these scenes are precise: she stammers, she touches her own hair, she stands slightly closer than the conversational norm, she laughs at jokes that aren't quite jokes. These are the markers of a child meeting a parent she has constructed in absentia.

**Phase 3 — Rupture (*Civil War II*, 2016).** Carol's predictive-justice crusade puts Kamala in the position of jailing innocents. The granular detail is critical: Kamala does not break with Carol *when she disagrees* — she follows for several issues past her own gut, because the trained behavior of the securely attached child is to assume the trusted authority figure has information she lacks. She breaks only when the cost becomes visible in faces she loves (Josh, Bruno). The break itself is silent — she does not confront Carol with a speech, she **leaves**. This is consistent with her general escalation pattern: she escalates toward self-erasure, not toward confrontation.

**Phase 4 — Flight (Karachi interval).** She physically removes herself from the relational field. Geographic distance is, for Kamala, the substitute for the relational rupture she cannot bring herself to enact verbally. Note the destination — not anywhere, but *family*. The wound from the idealized peer-authority is treated by returning to the secure base of blood relatives. This is textbook secure-attachment repair behavior: when the substitute object fails, return to origin.

**Phase 5 — Slow, incomplete repair.** Subsequent Carol appearances are correct but cool. The fan-postures (hair-touching, stammering, leaning-in) do not return. Kamala will fight alongside Carol, will save Carol, will accept Carol's apology in some panels — but the parasocial primary attachment is permanently downgraded to professional respect. **She has not, as of latest canon, fully metabolized this.** The dossier's standing prediction is that the next Carol-misstep will land with disproportionate force because Kamala is still carrying unmourned idealization of the earlier Carol.

This Carol arc is the **template** against which to read every other authority relationship she enters. She extends initial trust generously, follows past her own gut for one or two beats too long, breaks via withdrawal rather than confrontation, repairs through structural reform (the Champions are an *operational answer* to Carol's failure mode, not merely a new team), and never fully restores the original idealization.

## 6.4 The Bruno Carrelli Knot: Love, Obligation, and the Cripple-Guilt

Bruno is the most psychologically expensive relationship in Kamala's life. The structure is:

- **Childhood substrate.** They grew up together. The intimacy predates the possibility of romance, which means romance, when it arrives, arrives encrusted with sibling-feeling. This is a known relational trap and Kamala falls into it cleanly.
- **Asymmetric desire.** Bruno is in love with her. She knows. She does not reciprocate at the same temperature, and she also cannot cleanly refuse, because (a) she loves him truly, just not in that register, (b) her family/faith would not sanction the relationship anyway, which provides a convenient external veto she does not have to author, and (c) her own desire is genuinely ambivalent — there are panels (Wilson, mid-run) where she looks at Bruno with what is unmistakably romantic attention, and panels a chapter later where she does not.
- **The hand.** During *Civil War II*, Kamala's recklessness contributes to Bruno being maimed. His hand is permanently damaged. He moves to Wakanda. The departure is, from Kamala's interior, a banishment she imposed by being who she is.
- **The residue.** Every subsequent Bruno appearance carries this. She is over-careful with him. She over-apologizes for minor things, which is the displaced apology for the major thing she cannot find adequate words for. When Bruno returns and is dating Mike, Kamala's response is a textbook reaction-formation: she befriends Mike with conspicuous warmth, partly genuine, partly the performance of not-being-jealous as a way of avoiding examining whether she is.

**Generalization from the Bruno node:** Kamala's romantic-attachment style is **avoidant-with-guilt**. She loves easily and broadly but resists the specific configuration of pair-bonding, partly because her family/faith location gives her a permanent external script for deferral, and partly because — diagnostically — pair-bonding would require her to **be chosen as her singular self**, which is precisely the form of being-seen she most longs for and most fears. To be loved romantically is to be loved as Kamala Khan specifically — not as Carol's protégé, not as the perfect Muslim daughter, not as Ms. Marvel — and the prospect of receiving that and then losing it is, on the unconscious arithmetic, worse than not receiving it.

Note the Kareem (Red Dagger) variant — a permitted romantic interest (Pakistani, vaguely family-sanctioned, geographically distant) — which is the inverse permission structure: she can flirt because the geography makes consummation impossible. The *form* of the permission tells the truth about the avoidance.

## 6.5 The Champions Reformation: Building the Family She Designs

If the Avengers represent **inherited authority** and the Khan house represents **inherited love**, the Champions represent the **chosen family Kamala authored to her own specifications**. The team's founding charter — consent, transparency, no surveillance, no predictive coercion, peer accountability — is item-by-item the negative image of the *Civil War II* injuries. This is reform-by-construction, the most mature defense in her arsenal.

Within the Champions her relational pattern is:

- **Tactical co-leadership with Sam Alexander early on**; she defers the title but does the work, which is consistent with her chronic underclaiming.
- **Mentor-of-peers with Viv Vision and Riri Williams** — she becomes for them a version of the Carol-figure she lost, but configured around her revised theory of mentorship (no idealization invited, frequent self-deprecation, explicit invitations to disagree).
- **Sibling-coded warmth with Miles Morales and Amadeus Cho** — both are also children of immigrant communities, both also operate under bicultural identity loads, and the recognition is mutual and unspoken.

The Champions arc is also where her **messianic drift** becomes legible: when stressed, she slides toward the savior posture she critiqued in Carol. The pattern is recognizable to her teammates (Sam calls it out at least twice), and she corrects when called — which is itself the diagnostic difference from Carol. She can hear it.

## 6.6 The Granular Behavioral Tells of Bonding

Across the canon, Kamala's bonding behaviors are consistent enough to constitute a signature:

- **First-contact body language:** open hands, slight forward lean, fast smile, eye contact held one beat past Western neutral. She introduces herself with first name. She frequently makes a small self-deprecating joke within thirty seconds — the joke functions as a **trust-purchase**: she gives the other party permission to laugh at her, which is a low-cost gift that opens the channel.
- **Geek-shibboleth deployment:** she probes for fandom overlap (Avengers lore, sci-fi references, occasionally anime/games). When she finds overlap, the relational temperature jumps two clicks. When she doesn't, she adapts; she does not punish the absence.
- **Naming intimacy:** she gives or accepts nicknames quickly. "Bruno," "Nakia," "Zoe" — even authority figures get diminished registers eventually (Sheikh Abdullah is "Sheikh," Carol is "Carol" within four panels of meeting).
- **Physical proximity:** she stands closer than American norm to people she trusts, consistent with the South Asian family register she grew up in. She hugs without warning. She accepts hugs awkwardly when initiated by others — the asymmetry is telling.
- **The "abu" tell:** in moments of high emotion she occasionally code-switches into Urdu phrases, particularly with family and with Pakistani peers; the code-switch is involuntary and indexes safety.

## 6.7 Distrust Patterns

Distrust, when it arrives, is **slow, asymmetric, and structural rather than personal**.

She does not distrust individuals quickly. The Zoe Zimmer arc is diagnostic: Zoe is established as a casually racist mean-girl in issue 1, and over the run becomes one of Kamala's genuine friends. Kamala has *no apparent revenge instinct* and *no scorekeeping memory* about the earlier cruelty — she registers the change in Zoe and updates immediately. The same generosity is extended to Josh, to several early antagonists, to Loki (in crossovers), to Doc.X eventually.

She **does** distrust institutions, and that distrust is durable. The legal system (Kamala's Law), the predictive-policing infrastructure (*Civil War II*), the Inhuman political establishment (her wary relationship with Medusa), the carceral apparatus generally — these she will not extend benefit of the doubt to a second time once burned. The asymmetry is itself a tell: she has acquired a worldview in which **persons are redeemable and systems are not**, which is the precise inverse of the worldview that produces, for example, a Punisher.

The third axis of distrust is **self-distrust after moral failure**. Post-Bruno-hand, post-*Civil War II*, post-*Outlawed*, post-resurrection — each event triggers a period during which Kamala distrusts her own judgment specifically about the use of force and the assumption of authority. She does not distrust her values, only her competence to act on them. This produces the geographic-flight pattern (Karachi), the team-leaving pattern (Avengers exit), and the leadership-deferral pattern (Champions).

## 6.8 Betrayal and Repair

**How she is betrayed.** Almost exclusively by idealized authority (Carol) or by the institutionalization of her own image (Kamala's Law as the legal weaponization of her name). Peer betrayal is essentially absent from her canon — her friends do not turn on her. This is partly authorial, partly a function of the kind of community she selects for.

**How she repairs.** Slowly, asymmetrically, never via direct confrontation. Her repair toolkit:

1. **Geographic distance for cooling.** Karachi after *Civil War II*. Krakoa after resurrection. The space is not punishment; it is regulatory.
2. **Structural answer rather than verbal one.** The Champions are her sentence-length response to Carol's betrayal. The destruction of the Stormranger suit is her response to her own outsourced aggression. These are *actions* substituting for the conversations she does not have.
3. **Eventual partial return without restoration of original temperature.** She comes back. She works with Carol again. She is civil. She is not *fan* again.
4. **Internal re-articulation of principle.** After each major rupture, the canon shows her articulating, often in interior monologue or in conversation with Bruno or her father, the *principle* she has revised. This is the verbal labor she does in place of the confrontation.

**How she betrays.** She does, in fact, betray — primarily through over-functioning, recklessness, and the unilateral assumption that her judgment supersedes consent. Bruno's hand is the paradigm case: she did not ask him to participate at the cost he eventually paid. The *Outlawed* arc carries a smaller variant — she led underage heroes into a situation she could not control. The mature Kamala recognizes these as her characteristic failure mode, which is *messianic drift under stress*, and the Champions charter is in part her institutional firewall against her own tendency.

**How she is repaired by others.** Badly. She receives care with conspicuous awkwardness. Bruno taking care of her after an injury (multiple instances) is consistently followed by a self-deprecating deflection, a joke, a change of subject. Her parents fussing over her produces eye-rolls and squirming. The Champions checking in on her gets a brisk "I'm fine, focus." This is the **chronic-over-functioner's reception deficit**: she has built her identity around being the one who helps, and being helped destabilizes the self-concept. Notably, the people who succeed in caring for her are those who do so **without asking permission and without making it visible as care** — Yusuf bringing tea without comment, Bruno fixing her suit without being thanked, Sheikh Abdullah giving counsel disguised as a story. The successful caregivers in her life have learned to deliver care covertly.

## 6.9 The Repeated Relational Template

Aggregating across every major relationship — Carol, Bruno, Aamir, Yusuf, Muneeba, the Champions, the neighborhood, Kareem, Nakia, Zoe, Sheikh Abdullah, the X-Men post-resurrection — the same five-beat structure recurs:

1. **Open arrival.** She enters the relationship with hands up, fast smile, immediate first-name basis, a self-deprecating joke offered as a free gift.
2. **Generous incorporation.** She gives the other party the most flattering interpretation available. She over-credits, under-claims, integrates them into her existing social fabric within an issue or two.
3. **Over-functioning on their behalf.** She begins to take responsibility for their well-being beyond what the relationship requires. She schedules around them, defends them publicly, advocates structurally.
4. **Rupture by their failure or her error.** When the relationship is wounded, it is either because the other party (typically an authority) fails her morally, or because her over-functioning produces a cost she did not foresee and they paid. She does not rupture relationships through her own malice; she ruptures them through her own *excess*.
5. **Withdrawal-and-reform repair.** She does not confront. She withdraws — geographically, structurally, or somatically — and then returns with a quietly revised principle. The relationship resumes at a cooler, more honest temperature. She does not punish, but she also does not forget.

## 6.10 Dependency Pattern and Intimacy Architecture

She is **dependent on community in aggregate and independent in particular**. She needs the parish — the Jersey neighborhood, the family, the team, the mosque, the fandom — to function. Remove any one member and she compensates; remove the aggregate and she would collapse. She is not dependent on any single individual for emotional regulation, with the partial exception of her father, whose loss would be the catastrophic attachment injury her canon has not yet imposed.

Intimacy, in the dyadic sense, she keeps at the edge of arm's reach. The Bruno avoidance, the Kareem geographic-buffer, the absence of any sustained romantic partnership across nearly a decade of publication — these are not accidents of authorial pacing. They are the consistent output of an attachment system that **bonds easily to many and resists bonding deeply to one**, because the singular bond requires being seen as the singular self, and being seen as the singular self is precisely the wound and the wish she has not finished arbitrating.

The wager of her life, attachment-wise, is that she can substitute *breadth of bond* for *depth of singular bond* indefinitely. The dossier's standing prediction is that this wager will eventually be tested by an event — the loss of Yusuf, a serious romantic offer she cannot externally veto, the death of a Champion — that will force the dyadic intimacy she has spent her adolescence diversifying around. When it comes, she will have to choose, for the first time, whether to be **known by one person as her actual full plural self**. Her entire psychological architecture is, in a sense, in training for that test.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — KAMALA KHAN / MS. MARVEL
## SECTION: DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

A defensive architecture is a person's actual operating system, not their stated values. The subject's is unusually legible because she narrates it to herself out loud — in caption-box interior monologue, in text messages to Bruno, in muttered self-coaching mid-fight ("okay, okay, think, Kamala") — and because her power set externalizes psychic operations into visible morphology. When she dissociates, she literally grows. When she splits off her aggression, it walks around in a Kree nanosuit. When she wishes to be someone else, her cells comply. The file below catalogues the full stack, ordered from most primitive (Vaillant Level I, psychotic-adjacent and rare in her) up through immature (II), neurotic (III), to mature (IV), with attention to behavioral signature, somatic correlate, frequency, and trigger profile.

---

### I. PSYCHOTIC-LEVEL DEFENSES (Rare, Event-Locked)

The subject does not employ Level I defenses in baseline functioning. Two transient appearances merit notation.

**1. Denial (Frank, Reality-Distorting).** Observed in the immediate aftermath of her own death and resurrection. The subject returns to patrol, banter, and school with a velocity that is inconsistent with the magnitude of the event. This is not stoicism; stoicism acknowledges and elects to bear. The subject behaves as if the impalement did not occur to her — as if it happened to a previous draft of herself she has filed away. Behavioral tells: she does not visit the site, does not initiate conversation about the event, redirects sympathy ("I'm fine, seriously, can we talk about *anything* else"), and reports no nightmares on-page despite a sleep pattern that should produce them. The denial is partial — she knows it happened intellectually — but the affective register is absent. This is closer to **disavowal** than to true psychotic denial, and resolves into the more typical Level III avoidance suite within weeks.

**2. Delusional Projection (Sub-clinical, One-Time).** During the Doc.X / Kamala Korps arcs, her processing of being replicated/replaced contains a flickering near-belief that the duplicates are *her own externalized parts* — an idea the narrative entertains as metaphor but which the subject briefly entertains as fact. She recovers quickly. The episode is diagnostically inert but indicates that under sufficient identity-stress her reality-testing can momentarily soften at the seams.

---

### II. IMMATURE DEFENSES (Episodic, Stress-Locked)

These are the defenses that switch on when moral injury or somatic threat exceeds her Level III–IV capacity. They are not her resting state; they are her decompensation profile.

**3. Dissociation (Geographic and Somatic).** Her signature decompensation. The Karachi flight post–*Civil War II* is the textbook instance: she physically removes her body from the scene of the wound, ceases costume activity, refuses contact with American teammates, and re-enters her childhood self by occupying her childhood relatives' household. This is not vacation; it is a re-located self. Somatic correlate: during the flight period her morphic discipline relaxes, she sleeps differently, eats differently, dresses differently. Lesser episodes: micro-dissociations during the post-resurrection interval, where she will "go quiet" mid-conversation, the eyes glazing for half a beat before the smile reboots.
