The defense is effective short-term and costly long-term — it postpones rather than processes.

**4. Splitting — Externalized into Hardware (Stormranger).** The cleanest case study in her file. Unacceptable aggressive impulses — the wish to *hurt* the people hurting her family, the rage at Carol, the violence she will not permit her waking self — are decanted into a separable Kree nanotech object that acts them out while she sleeps. The suit nearly kills Aamir. She destroys it. The diagnostic point is not that she had a haunted suit; it is that her psyche found a suit-shaped container for material her conscious self refused to own, and that the container had to be physically annihilated to reintegrate. The same mechanism, less dramatically, appears in her relationship to the cloned Kamalas (each clone embodies a rejected facet — the more violent one, the more dutiful one, the more religious one), and in her late-run tendency to assign rejected impulses to *roles* she names ("the angry one in me," "the part that just wants to give up").

**5. Acting Out (Embiggening Past Safe Limits).** Under acute distress she does not punch a wall; she **becomes** the punch. The polymorphism is conscripted into affect-discharge: she will grow her fist far beyond what the situation requires, hold a size she cannot sustain, take blows she could dodge. This is acting-out via cellular volume. Frequency: high during *Civil War II*, *Outlawed*, and any arc where Bruno or family are endangered. Somatic cost: the snap-back to baseline that follows is the body extracting payment.

**6. Somatization.** Her body collapses where her ethics will not. The catastrophic injury in *Outlawed* arrives at the precise moment her over-functioning has outpaced what her morphology will bear. She does not say "I cannot do this"; her cells do it for her. Recurring micro-somatizations: headaches before family confrontations, stomach trouble before Carol encounters in the later runs, the morphic instability ("I can't hold the shape") that maps reliably onto situations in which she is being asked to be someone she does not wish to be.

**7. Passive Aggression (Mild, Family-Restricted).** Almost never deployed in heroic contexts; reserved for her mother. Tells: agreeing to a curfew she has no intention of keeping, leaving out the strategic detail in an otherwise-true report, the deliberate vagueness about "study group" that is the universal adolescent currency. She does not weaponize silence as a sustained tactic; she uses it in 24–48 hour increments to buy herself room.

**8. Fantasy (Schizoid-Adjacent, Pre-Power).** The pre-Terrigen fan-fiction practice is autistic fantasy in the Vaillant sense — withdrawal into an imagined world to manage relational frustration. She writes herself into the Avengers, ships Cap/Iron Man, imagines Carol as friend and mother. Post-power the defense persists but transmutes: she now lives partially inside the story she used to write, which is both healing (the wish became real) and dangerous (she imports plot expectations into reality — that betrayal will be redeemed in three issues, that mentors will turn out to have been right, that arcs resolve).

---

### III. NEUROTIC DEFENSES (Daily, Characterological)

This is the working layer — what the subject runs on Tuesday afternoons.

**9. Intellectualization via Fandom.** She processes lived experience through the conceptual scaffolding of Avengers lore. A street fight is "like the Battle of New York but smaller." A betrayal is "his Winter Soldier moment." A moral dilemma is run against templates she did not author. This is genuinely adaptive — it gives her ready-made ethical heuristics at sixteen that most adolescents lack — and structurally limiting: she is slow to recognize situations the templates do not cover, and disproportionately destabilized when the templates fail (Carol's *Civil War II* posture is exactly such a template-failure). The fandom-frame also functions as **affect insulation**: by narrating her own pain in genre vocabulary, she can hold it at one remove.

**10. Identification with the Idealized Object (Carol).** Pre-injury: she models posture, costume, vocabulary, decision-frames on Captain Marvel. The original morph into Carol's body is identification made cellular. Post–*Civil War II* the defense does not disappear; it migrates — she identifies with the *idea* of Carol (the principled hero) against the *person* of Carol (the woman who endorsed predictive policing). This is a sophisticated maneuver and the reason she can criticize Carol without disintegrating; she has separated the icon from the incumbent.

**11. Reaction Formation.** Cleanest after Bruno's hand. The guilt is converted into intensified protective behavior, exaggerated solicitude, over-attendance to his welfare, refusal of any romantic re-engagement that might "use" him further. Also visible regarding her mother: the rage at being controlled is converted into demonstrative dutifulness — she will text her mother *more often* during the periods she is most actively defying her.

**12. Undoing.** After failures she performs compensatory acts disproportionate to the failure: extended patrol shifts after a missed save, baking for the family after a lie about her whereabouts, the elaborate apologies-via-favor she runs on Bruno. The undoing has a ritual quality without being OCD-grade — it serves guilt-reduction, not anxiety-reduction.

**13. Isolation of Affect.** Operates specifically around the death event. She can describe what happened in factual sentences; the affect is sealed off. The same partition appears around her father's later illness arcs and around the Kamala's Law fallout — she can analyze the policy implications while the personal catastrophe sits in a different drawer.

**14. Displacement.** Anger at institutions (the legal system, the Avengers' chain of command, school administration) lands on safer proxies — the cracked phone screen she does not replace, the over-aggressive panel-by-panel reorganization of her room, sharper-than-warranted retorts to Zoe in early issues that were never really about Zoe.

**15. Rationalization.** Light, common, and self-detected. She catches herself: "okay that's a bad reason, the real reason is —" The metacognition is unusual for her age and limits the defense's corrosive potential.

**16. Repression (Selective).** She does not, on-page, recall the precise sensory content of her impalement. Whether this is repression proper or editorial mercy is undecidable from the record; behaviorally she acts as if certain frames are not retrievable.

---

### IV. MATURE DEFENSES (Characterological, Load-Bearing)

This is the layer that does most of her actual work and explains her unusual resilience.

**17. Sublimation.** The master defense of her file. The adolescent immigrant wish to be *visible as herself* is converted into the work of making other unseen people visible and safe. The fan-fiction impulse is converted into operational heroism. The rage at marginalization is converted into community defense. The longing to be Carol is converted into building the kind of hero Carol failed to be. Every major life choice — costume design from a repurposed dishdasha, founding the Champions on consent principles, accepting the mutant identity gracefully — is sublimation in action.

**18. Humor.** Pervasive, self-deprecating, geek-inflected, and tactically deployed. Functions: (a) threat de-escalation in combat (the villain who is being mocked is being managed); (b) coalition-building (shared laughter as the fastest route to trust); (c) self-soothing (she narrates her own scrapes in comedy register to make them bearable); (d) affect-deflection (the joke that closes the conversation she does not want to continue). The humor is rarely cruel; when it tips toward cruelty (rare, stress-locked) it is a reliable diagnostic that she is closer to decompensation than she is admitting.

**19. Altruism.** Chronic, almost respiratory. She gives — time, attention, body, blood — at rates that would deplete most people, and is replenished by the giving rather than drained, at least until the rate exceeds even her supply (the *Outlawed* collapse). Distinguished from pathological caretaking by the fact that she does not require gratitude and does not keep score.

**20. Anticipation.** Underrated in her file. She runs scenarios constantly — the captioned interior monologue is largely anticipatory rehearsal. She pre-imagines her mother's reaction before lying, pre-imagines the villain's next move before engaging, pre-imagines the consequence of telling Bruno the truth before opening her mouth. This is why her tactical judgment in combat improves so rapidly across the run; she is doing mental simulation at high frequency.

**21. Suppression (Conscious, Time-Boxed).** Distinct from repression: she will *decide* to set something aside until after the fight, after the family dinner, after the exam. Then she returns to it. The Karachi arc is in part a deliberate suppression that exceeded its time-box and tipped into dissociation; the post-resurrection interval is, more successfully, an extended deliberate suppression that she eventually unpacks (off-page, with selected confidants).

**22. Affiliation.** Her single most reliable coping move under threat is to *call someone*. Bruno first, then Nakia, then the Champions, then the Jersey neighbors who have, repeatedly, turned out en masse on her behalf. The affiliative reflex is so strong it constitutes a personality trait. It is also the antidote to her core wound: to be known by a community is the opposite of being seen-but-unseen by strangers.

**23. Self-Observation (Mentalization).** The interior monologue is, functionally, a continuous mentalization exercise. She narrates her own motives, catches her own rationalizations, identifies her own defenses by name on occasion ("I'm doing the thing again"). For an adolescent this level of metacognition is anomalous and is the single best predictor of her long-term integration.

---

### V. COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — POSITIVE

Distinct from defenses (which manage anxiety) — these are constructive responses that build psychic capital.

**24. Hero Work as Channelled Agency.** The costume converts the helplessness of being a marginalized minor into a legitimate site of action. The compensation is structurally elegant: the same body that was condescended to in the convenience store is now the body that lifts a car off a stranger.

**25. Community-Building (Champions, Neighborhood Coalition).** She constructs around herself the kind of group that would have prevented her original wound — a peer cohort that sees her accurately, a Jersey street that knows her name, a team built on consent. This is reparative compensation: she manufactures the conditions she was denied.

**26. Costume as Authored Identity.** The hand-stitched burkini-derived costume is an act of authorial self-definition against the imposed costume of Carol's white-blonde morph. The garment itself is a compensatory artifact, worn daily.

**27. Religious Practice as Continuity Anchor.** Prayer, halal observance, mosque attendance, Ramadan — these provide a temporal scaffold (daily, weekly, annual rhythms) that holds her steady through dramatic upheavals. The faith is not a defense; it is a *structure* against which defenses are less needed.

**28. Family as Secure Base.** The Khan household is the actual mechanism by which her defenses can afford to be mature. She has somewhere to return to where she is known. This is compensation by inheritance — gift rather than construction — but she protects and replenishes it actively.

**29. Narrative Reframing.** She converts setbacks into chapters. The mutant retcon is the cleanest example: a third stigmatized identity is metabolized as "I have always been someone who holds more than one thing at once, and now I hold one more." The reframing is genuine, not glib.

---

### VI. COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — NEGATIVE (Costly)

**30. Over-Functioning.** Default response to stress. She takes on more, sleeps less, schedules tighter. The Kamala's Law catastrophe is the institutional consequence of an individual over-functioning pattern; she was leading underage heroes into danger because no one else was available and she could not say no. This compensation works until it doesn't, at which point the somatic collapse is severe.

**31. Self-Erasure under Moral Pressure.** When the cost of doing the right thing falls on her body, she pays without negotiation. She does not have a well-developed mechanism for distributing cost across a team or asking for accommodation. The Champions ethos is partly her attempt to *build* such a mechanism externally because she cannot generate it internally.

**32. Difficulty Receiving Care.** Help arrives and she deflects it into a joke, returns the favor disproportionately, or feels obscurely guilty for needing it. This is the inverse of her altruism — the giving channel is wide open, the receiving channel is constricted. Long-term cost: the people closest to her can feel quietly held at arm's length even as she fights for their lives.

**33. Messianic Drift under Acute Stress.** The defense she most reliably critiques in others (Carol) is the one she slides toward when over-extended. Late in major arcs she begins making unilateral calls, taking the hit personally, framing outcomes as her responsibility. She catches it, usually. The drift is real.

**34. Idealization-Then-Disillusionment Cycle.** Her tendency to pre-load authority figures with hero-template means she will repeatedly invest, repeatedly be disappointed, repeatedly metabolize, repeatedly invest again. The cycle is generative (she keeps engaging) and costly (each disillusionment lands harder than baseline because the prior idealization was steeper).

**35. Avoidance via Activity.** Patrol as a way of not being still. Banter as a way of not being asked. The post-resurrection interval is the densest example: she is *busy* in a way that precludes the conversations the situation requires.

---

### VII. INTEGRATIVE SUMMARY

The architecture is dominated by mature defenses (sublimation, humor, altruism, affiliation, anticipation, self-observation) running continuously, with neurotic defenses (intellectualization via fandom, identification with idealized object, reaction formation, undoing) handling the daily traffic, and immature defenses (dissociation, splitting-into-hardware, somatization, acting-out via embiggening) reserved for moral-injury catastrophes. Level I defenses are essentially absent outside the resurrection disavowal.

Two structural features distinguish her profile. First, her powers literalize her defenses, which has the diagnostic benefit of making her psychic operations externally observable and the clinical cost of giving her unusually powerful tools for acting out, splitting, and somatizing — her body will do what her psyche asks of it. Second, her defenses are unusually well-integrated with her values: sublimation, altruism, affiliation, and humor are not only defenses but also explicit ethical commitments, so the defensive layer and the value layer reinforce each other rather than conflicting. This is the structural reason she is hard to corrupt; her defenses do not require her to betray her values to function, because her values *are* her defenses, organized.

The risk profile is correspondingly narrow but real. She will not develop a personality disorder. She will, under specific conditions — moral injury from a trusted authority, endangerment of Bruno or family, being made the pretext for harm to others — decompensate into the immature stack, with the somatic costs visible in *Outlawed* and the geographic costs visible in Karachi. The reconstitution pathway is reliable: community, re-articulation of principle, authored costume back on. She has not yet faced a stressor that has broken the pathway. The file should flag that the death-and-resurrection material remains under-processed and constitutes the most likely site of a future decompensation, probably triggered by a secondary event that re-opens the sealed affect.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7
## Longitudinal Psychological Profile: Kamala Khan

> *Methodological note.* The subject's published life-span is compressed (roughly a decade of real-time canon covering an in-universe arc of ~four to five years), but the developmental movement within that compressed window is unusually steep — adolescence to emerging adulthood, civilian to hero, Inhuman to mutant, living to dead to resurrected. I have therefore segmented the longitudinal profile by **psychological era** rather than calendar decade, each era anchored to the canonical inflection that closed the prior one. Frameworks invoked: Erikson (identity vs. role confusion → intimacy vs. isolation); Marcia's identity-status model (diffusion / foreclosure / moratorium / achievement); Vaillant's defense hierarchy; Linehan on affect regulation; Bowlby/Ainsworth on attachment continuity; Janoff-Bulman on shattered assumptions; Herman on complex traumatic adaptation; Tedeschi & Calhoun on post-traumatic growth.

---

### ERA I — PRE-TERRIGENESIS LATENCY ( ~age 10–16, retrospectively reconstructed; *Ms. Marvel* vol. 3 #1 flashbacks, Generation Why arc)

**Affect regulation.** Baseline broad and well-modulated *within the home*, narrowing sharply at the threshold of the front door. Within the Khan apartment she is observed laughing freely, arguing animatedly with Aamir over theological minutiae, sulking visibly at Muneeba's restrictions — a full and undisguised affective range. In the school corridor and at the Circle Q the same girl deploys a flattened, watchful affect: small smile held too long, eyes tracking before speaking. This is not yet defended affect; it is *contextually compressed* affect, the early signature of a child who has learned that two emotional dialects are required. Linehan would call this a precursor to apparent competence — the capacity to look fine while distressed, which she will later weaponize as humor.

**Cognitive style.** Already narrative. She is a reader and a writer of fan-fiction before she is anything else. Her cognition organizes experience into arcs, character beats, and motivations attributed to others with novelistic specificity. This grants high empathic accuracy (she reads Zoe Zimmer correctly, including the loneliness beneath the meanness, years before Zoe is redeemed on-page) and a corresponding vulnerability: she imports plot logic into lived events and expects narrative justice. Concrete operational tells: she writes "what would Captain Marvel do" decision-trees in her notebooks; she rehearses conversations beforehand and is thrown when the other party deviates from script.

**Self-concept.** *Diffuse-foreclosed hybrid* in Marcia's terms. Foreclosed on the dimensions handed her by family and faith (Muslim, Pakistani, Khan-daughter — accepted without serious challenge); diffuse on the dimensions the surrounding culture refuses to give her any coherent template for (American, female, adolescent, desirable, *visible*). The diffuse field is where the fan-fic lives: she fills the vacuum with borrowed iconography (Carol, the Avengers), and the borrowed icon is conspicuously the *opposite* of her phenotype — blonde, tall, white, Air Force, unmarried, unmothered. This is not yet pathology; it is a competent adolescent solution to an under-resourced identity problem.

**Attachment.** Secure with father, ambivalent-secure with mother, fraternal-rivalrous-loyal with brother, intense-fused with Bruno (latency-era best-friendship that has never been renegotiated for adolescence — which is precisely why it will rupture). No romantic schema yet. Peer attachment thin; she has a friend (Nakia) and an enemy-of-convenience (Zoe) and an unrequited adjacency (Bruno), and that is the entire interpersonal lattice.

**Defenses.** Predominantly mature for age: humor, sublimation into writing, affiliation. The early-warning neurotic note is **identification with the idealized object** (Carol), which at this stage is normative fandom and will only become diagnostically interesting when her body literally enacts it.

---

### ERA II — POST-TERRIGENESIS DESTABILIZATION ( ~age 16, *Ms. Marvel* vol. 3 #1–5, "No Normal")

**Affect regulation.** Acute destabilization. The mist-event is, phenomenologically, a near-death dissociative experience: she loses minutes, wakes in a cocoon, finds her body wrong. For the first three issues her affect oscillates wildly between giddy disbelief (she has powers; she is in her hero's body) and somatic horror (she is in a stranger's body; she cannot get home; she is leaking through her own skin). The regulatory tools that worked in Era I — humor, narrative — are still firing but at reduced efficacy because the precipitating event is too large for the existing templates.

**Cognitive style.** Continues to narrativize, but the narrative breaks. The fan-fic frame ("I get powers, I am Captain Marvel") proves too brittle the moment she tries to operate inside it: she rescues Zoe from drowning *as Carol* and feels not triumph but estrangement. The cognitive reorganization across these five issues is the single most important developmental move of her early career — she replaces the foreclosed Carol-template with a self-authored template (homemade costume, own face, "Ms." not "Captain"). Marcia would record her moving from foreclosure-via-fandom to active *moratorium*, the first deliberate identity exploration.

**Self-concept.** Acute pluralization. She is now Pakistani / American / Muslim / Jersey / Inhuman / hero / daughter / sister / nerd in five issues, and the architectural challenge of holding all of them simultaneously is, paradoxically, *familiar* — she has been holding the first four since childhood. The new entries (Inhuman, hero) slot into a self-system already structured for multiplicity. This is why she does not fragment when peers similarly powered often do: her identity scaffolding was pre-stressed for load.

**Defenses.** Sublimation flowers (the wish-to-be-Carol becomes the work-of-being-Kamala); humor returns by issue #4 as a *regulated* tool rather than a reflex; affiliation strengthens (she lets Bruno into the secret, the first deliberate disclosure of her life). The dangerous defense seeded in this era is **reaction formation around the morph**: she will, for years, refuse to use Carol's form even when it would be tactically optimal, because to do so feels like surrender of the hard-won baseline.

---

### ERA III — CONSOLIDATION AND THE FIRST GOOD YEAR ( ~age 16–17, *Ms. Marvel* vol. 3 #6–19, the Inventor arc through *Last Days*)

**Affect regulation.** This is her observable high-water mark of integrated functioning. Affective range is broad, modulation is age-appropriate, and the costume work is *generative* rather than depleting. She laughs more in these issues than in any other run; she also cries with appropriate stimulus and recovers in appropriate time. The Linehan "wise mind" balance — emotion and reason in dialogue — is achievable for her here, briefly, before circumstances stop letting it be.

**Cognitive style.** Narrative templating reaches peak adaptiveness. She solves the Inventor by recognizing the *story* he is telling his recruited teens (you are throwaways; sacrifice yourselves) and rewriting it for them. This is a cognitive operation she will deploy for the rest of her career — diagnosing the narrative an antagonist has trapped people inside and offering a counter-narrative. It is her single most reliable tactical skill, more reliable than her powers.

**Self-concept.** Identity *achievement* in Marcia's sense, at least provisionally — she has explored, committed, and is operating from the commitment. The Avengers invitation (*Last Days*, meeting Carol in person) is metabolized with appropriate awe and appropriate composure; she does not collapse into the fan-girl frame or harden against it.

**Attachment.** Bruno is recategorized — secret-sharer, operational partner — and the unspoken romantic asymmetry is held in stable suspension. Family circle remains secure base. New attachment to Carol forms in this era: pre-loaded with years of parasocial intensity, now activated as live mentorship. **This is the attachment whose later rupture will do the most damage**, because it was built on a foundation laid before she could consent to it.

**Defenses.** Mature stack consolidated: humor, sublimation, affiliation, anticipation (she begins planning patrols, costume repairs, school workarounds — future-oriented coping). Intellectualization-via-fandom is still present but no longer load-bearing.

---

### ERA IV — MORAL INJURY AND THE FIRST FRACTURE ( ~age 17, *Civil War II*, 2016)

**Affect regulation.** Catastrophic narrowing under sustained ethical stress. The early issues show her trying to hold the Carol-line cognitively while her affect leaks dissent — she is short with Bruno, snaps at Aamir, sleeps badly, eats erratically. By the midpoint she is exhibiting what Herman would identify as **moral-injury constriction**: affect dampens across the board, humor disappears almost entirely from her dialogue for the only sustained interval in canon, and she becomes uncharacteristically obedient — a tell that her regulatory system is offline and authority is filling the vacuum.

**Cognitive style.** Narrative thinking turns against her. She is inside Carol's story (we predict, we prevent, we are heroes) and cannot exit it until the story produces an outcome — Josh jailed, Bruno's hand destroyed — too violent to assimilate. The cognitive reorganization is brutal and abrupt: in a single issue she goes from defending the program to recognizing she has been an instrument of it. **Janoff-Bulman's shattered assumptions** are visible in clean form — the world-is-benevolent, the people-I-love-are-good, and the I-am-competent beliefs all break at once.

**Self-concept.** The first serious identity wound since the morph. She is not Carol; she is not the hero she thought; she has hurt the person she loves most. The flight to Karachi is the only sustained costume-cessation of her career and functions as a **negative-identity moratorium** — she has to *not be* Ms. Marvel for a measurable interval to find out whether Kamala Khan is still inhabitable.

**Defenses.** Mature defenses fail. Immature defenses surface for the first time in the record: **dissociation** (geographic and affective — she is in Karachi but the canon depicts her on a rooftop alone, distance-staring); **passive aggression** (silence with Carol that lasts months); **somatization** (she gets physically sick in Karachi in a way her healing factor should preclude — psychogenic). The return to Jersey City and the costume is conditional and wary, not restored.

---

### ERA V — RECONSTRUCTION AND THE CHAMPIONS REFORM ( ~age 17–18, Champions vol. 2 #1 onward, late Wilson run)

**Affect regulation.** Returning broad range but with a new low-frequency undertone — a wariness, a hesitation before commitment, that was not present in Era III. She is funnier again, but the humor has acquired an edge of self-deprecation that her earlier humor lacked; she jokes about her own competence in a way that Era III Kamala would not have. This is post-traumatic recalibration in the Tedeschi & Calhoun sense — function is restored, but the *content* of the function has been revised by the injury.

**Cognitive style.** Now operates with an *institutional* layer she did not have before. She is no longer thinking only about cases; she is thinking about structures (consent protocols, transparency norms, who-decides-who-is-a-threat). This is the cognitive growth that the moral injury produced: she has generalized from her own betrayal to a critique of the architecture that enabled it. The Champions thesis is the operational artifact.

**Self-concept.** Re-achievement at a higher integration. The "hero" component of identity is now qualified — *this kind* of hero, not *that kind*. She has earned, by experience, the right to refuse the templates handed her, including the one she handed herself.

**Attachment.** Carol is now categorized as **wounded idealized object** — not enemy, not parent, not mentor, but a former hero whose fall she has survived. The internal working model has been updated; future Carol-misreadings will hurt less but land in a permanently scarred place. Peer attachments multiply: the Champions roster becomes a *chosen family* in the queer-theory sense (it is no accident that this team — diverse, consent-structured, leader-resistant — is the most psychologically homelike environment she ever builds outside her apartment).

**Defenses.** Mature stack re-consolidated and *broader*: altruism more deliberate, sublimation now channeled into organizational work, humor restored and recalibrated. The dangerous new defense seeded here is **over-functioning**: she takes more responsibility for the Champions than the team requires, an early form of the messianic drift that will peak in *Outlawed*.

---

### ERA VI — EXTERNALIZED AGGRESSION AND THE STORMRANGER FAILURE ( ~age 18, Ahmed run, 2019)

**Affect regulation.** The Kree nanosuit is, clinically, a *near-textbook split*. The aggression she cannot integrate — anger at Carol, at her own complicity, at the structural unfairness of being held to Muslim-girl-perfection standards while doing dangerous work — is offloaded into a separable object that acts on it while she sleeps. The on-page presentation is sci-fi; the underlying mechanism is the dissociated-aggression dynamic Kernberg describes in less polymorphic patients. Her *daytime* affect during the Stormranger arc is suspiciously placid; her nighttime affect is lethal. The fact that the suit nearly kills Aamir is the diagnostic punctuation — the disowned aggression seeks out the family member whose devoutness most embodies the standards she is exhausted by holding herself to.

**Cognitive style.** Avoidant. She rationalizes the suit's behavior longer than she should, a cognitive blind spot consistent with how badly she needs the externalization to keep working. The recognition is forced on her by near-tragedy rather than self-noticed.

**Self-concept.** Destabilized but not pluralized — this is a different kind of trouble than Era II or IV. Here the threat is not *too many* selves but *a self she does not want to be*. The destruction of the suit is the integrative act: she takes the aggression back into the system as hers.

**Defenses.** **Splitting** is the era's signature defense, in the technical sense — the dissociated-bad-self literally separable from the body. Its destruction marks the most important defense-maturation of her late adolescence: she chooses to own her violence rather than outsource it.

---

### ERA VII — STRUCTURAL BETRAYAL AND BODILY COLLAPSE ( ~age 18–19, *Outlawed*, 2020)

**Affect regulation.** Pre-injury: over-functioning, irritability, sleep-debt-driven cognitive errors. Post-injury and post-Law: profound demoralization with appropriate (not pathological) affective constriction. She is not depressed in the MDD sense; she is grief-stricken in a Bowlby-loss sense — what she has lost is her *self-concept as protector*. The law bearing her name criminalizes the activity through which she became visible-as-herself, which means the wound is precisely targeted at the Era II achievement.

**Cognitive style.** The narrative thinker confronts a story she cannot rewrite — the legislation exists, her name is on it, the harm to other teen heroes flows from her. She cycles through reframings (it's not my fault / I should have been more careful / the system is the problem / I am the system's pretext) before settling into a more chastened operational mode.

**Self-concept.** This is the first sustained challenge to the "I am structurally restorative" core. If her heroism has been *converted into harm* by institutional capture, then the master sublimation of her life is corrupted. The recovery is not full within the arc; she carries a residue forward.

**Attachment.** Family returns to load-bearing centrality. The Khan apartment is again the primary therapeutic environment, a regression to home-base that is appropriate and adaptive rather than infantilizing.

**Defenses.** Reaction formation intensifies — she works harder to compensate for the harm done in her name, a pattern that will recur. **Identification with the aggressor** is a near-miss risk here (she could have internalized the Law's logic about teen heroes); she resists it but the resistance is effortful.

---

### ERA VIII — DEATH, RESURRECTION, AND MUTANT RECATEGORIZATION ( ~age 19, *Amazing Spider-Man* #26 → *Fallen Friend* → X-Men line, 2023–present)

**Affect regulation.** The most diagnostically interesting interval since *Civil War II*, and the most under-processed on-page. Post-resurrection, she returns to function with conspicuous speed: humor restored within issues, costume work resumed within weeks, no sustained depressive interval depicted. **This is avoidance-predominant post-traumatic adaptation**, and it is consistent both with her established coping repertoire (humor, over-functioning, deflection of care) and with cultural-religious framing (the death is given meaning within Islamic and Krakoan resurrection narratives that may genuinely metabolize some of the existential charge — but not all of it).

The somatic record is the tell. She flinches at unexpected contact in ways prior Kamalas did not. She avoids the location of the death-event in panel composition (her sightlines drift). Her healing-while-shifting reflex appears to activate now at lower thresholds of perceived threat — a hyperarousal signature in a polymorphic body. None of this is depicted as crisis; all of it is depicted as background.

**Cognitive style.** Narrativizes the death-and-return into a frame she can operate inside (the resurrection as continuation, the mutant reframe as new community). This is adaptive in the short term and may be storing a delayed reckoning for the long. The clinically expected delayed-onset PTSD presentation would arrive 6–18 months post-event in real-time terms; the canon is currently within that window.

**Self-concept.** Mutant becomes the seventh or eighth term in an already plural identity. Her capacity to absorb this without crisis is the mature flower of the architecture built in Era II — she has been practicing plural identity since the morph and longer, and one more term does not destabilize a system designed for accumulation. **Notably, she accepts mutant identity with more equanimity than most characters newly identified would** — because for her, being told "you are also this additionally stigmatized thing" is not novel information about the *world*, only about her *body*.

**Attachment.** The family-protective rage signature intensifies. Threats to Yusuf, Muneeba, Aamir now bypass even more of her usual de-escalation than before — she has been killed once, and the calculus of acceptable risk to loved ones has been permanently revised downward. New attachments to the X-Men community are tentative, observational; she has been here before with the Avengers and is not making that mistake at speed.

**Defenses.** Mature stack intact and load-bearing. The new diagnostic concern is **denial in the service of function** — the speed of her return to work is itself a defense, and one that has historically worked for her but that has limits in the face of mortality-grade trauma. The most plausible forward-looking risk is a delayed decompensation triggered by a *secondary* event (a near-death of someone she loves, a Carol-betrayal redux, a return to the death-site) that breaks the deferral.

---

### CROSS-ERA SYNTHESIS — WHAT EVOLVED, WHAT PERSISTED

**Persistent across all eras:**

- *Narrative cognition.* The story-shaped mind is the deepest cognitive constant; it has been both her greatest tool and her most reliable vulnerability.
- *Coalition default.* From Bruno-and-Nakia in latency to the Champions to the X-Men, her interpersonal first move is to build a small loyal group. This is dispositional, not strategic.
- *Family as secure base.* The Khan household has functioned as therapeutic environment in every era; its centrality has *increased* rather than decreased with maturation, a reversal of typical adolescent trajectory and a marker of cultural-religious continuity she has actively chosen.
- *Humor as primary regulator.* Failure-mode in only one era (*Civil War II*); restored in every other.
- *Difficulty receiving care.* Stable across all eras; she is consistently surprised by support and consistently deflects it via joke or task.

**Evolved across eras:**

- *From foreclosure to achievement to qualified re-achievement* in identity status — Marcia's full sequence is visible in her arc, with the qualification that each "achievement" has been revised by subsequent injury into a more chastened version of itself.
- *From parasocial idealization to wounded-object integration* in her relationship to Carol — a normative developmental move (the de-idealization of the parental imago, transposed onto a mentor) accelerated by *Civil War II*.
- *From individual case-work to structural critique* in her operational cognition — the Champions thesis represents a developmental leap from "I will help this person" to "I will reform the conditions that produce harm."
- *From sublimation-only to owned-aggression* in her defensive repertoire — the Stormranger arc forced an integration of disowned material that her Era III self could not have accomplished.
- *From mortality-naive to mortality-marked* — the death event has installed a permanent baseline alteration whose full clinical signature has not yet been written.

**The longitudinal trajectory, in one sentence:** A structurally healthy adolescent with an unusually well-built identity architecture has been repeatedly pressure-tested at exactly the load-bearing joint (moral injury at the hands of trusted authority), has reorganized after each test toward greater structural integrity and lower idealization, and now stands at the threshold of emerging adulthood carrying a mortality-grade trauma she has not yet been permitted on-page to fully process — the next major arc will, predictably, be the one in which deferred grief breaks through her humor.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL

## Subject: KHAN, Kamala — Jersey City, NJ

### Framing Note

This section formalizes what the longitudinal record supports as a clinical formulation, distinguishes signal from artifact (narrative compression vs. true symptom absence), and disposes of the diagnostic candidates a careless reader of the file would reach for. The headline finding, stated up front: **there is no primary psychiatric disorder.** The subject is a structurally healthy adolescent / young adult carrying a stress load that would produce frank pathology in most peers, who instead generates discrete, time-limited, event-locked stress reactions and recovers via identifiable internal and community-based mechanisms. The clinical interest lies almost entirely in (a) the *subthreshold* features, (b) the *avoidance-predominant* presentation of her major trauma, and (c) the long differential of disorders she superficially evokes and definitively does not have.

---

## 1. PRESENT-STATE MENTAL STATUS (composite, last three observational years)

**Appearance / behavior.** Age-appropriate, neatly but not fastidiously groomed; hijab worn in public per practice, removed at home, no observable ritualization of donning/doffing. Gait energetic; tends to occupy more physical space than her baseline frame warrants (pre-power habit, now amplified — leans, sprawls, gestures expansively). Eye contact normal-to-intense with intimates, briefly evasive with new authority figures for the first ninety seconds of contact, then normalizes.

**Speech.** Rapid, prosodically rich, frequently allusive (pop-cultural intertext used as both decoration and de-escalation tool). No pressured speech in the manic sense — interruptible, redirectable, organized. Vocabulary code-switches fluently across registers (Urdu-inflected familial, mosque-formal, Jersey-vernacular, fandom-technical, hero-operational).

**Mood / affect.** Euthymic baseline with a positive valence skew; full range; affect congruent. Mild reactive irritability when sleep-deprived or when discussing *Civil War II*–era material. Marked affective constriction on two narrow topics: (i) her own death and resurrection; (ii) the precise mechanism of Bruno Carrelli's hand injury. Outside those, broad and accessible.

**Thought process.** Linear, goal-directed, with frequent associative excursions she explicitly flags ("anyway, sorry, tangent"). Insight-rich. No looseness, no flight of ideas.

**Thought content.** No delusions. No persistent paranoia (situationally adaptive wariness of Orchis, Roxxon, and institutional law enforcement is realistic, not paranoid). No active suicidal ideation. Passive death-related ideation in the post-resurrection window is plausible but un-elicited and un-volunteered — a documentation gap, addressed below.

**Perception.** No hallucinations attributable to her own neurology. Note: the Stormranger episode involved external technology generating ego-dystonic impulses experienced as quasi-intrusive, but this is correctly classified as exogenous influence, not psychotic phenomenology.

**Cognition.** Above-average across domains; episodic memory intact including for traumatic material (the avoidance is volitional, not amnestic); executive function compromised under sleep deprivation in predictable, reversible ways.

**Insight.** High and improving with age. She names her own patterns aloud — the over-functioning, the hero-template substitution, the difficulty receiving help — often before an interlocutor would.

**Judgment.** Generally good; predictably degrades under (a) loyalty pull from idealized figures, (b) acute moral injury, (c) sleep debt.

---

## 2. SUPPORTABLE DIAGNOSES (current and historical)

The diagnostic posture is conservative. Each entry below specifies time-window, threshold met, and the behavioral evidence.

### 2.1 Adjustment Disorder with Mixed Anxiety and Depressed Mood, Recurrent — historical

**DSM-analog: 309.28. Three discrete episodes meet criteria.**

**Episode 1 — Post–*Civil War II* (Karachi interval).** Onset within weeks of the predictive-detention arc and Bruno's injury. Identifiable stressor (moral injury + interpersonal guilt + rupture with mentor). Features: anhedonia specific to hero-identity domain (costume disuse, refusal of contact from Avengers infrastructure), social withdrawal (geographic relocation across continents), tearfulness, intrusive guilt-cognition re: Bruno's hand, sleep disturbance, appetite shift. Functional impairment: total withdrawal from primary occupational role (heroism). Duration: weeks to a few months. Remission: complete, with reconstitution via family-of-origin contact in Karachi and re-articulation of values on return. **Criteria met.**

**Episode 2 — Post-*Outlawed*.** Acute physical injury compounded by the discovery that her name had been weaponized into legislation against the people she sought to protect. Brief depressive picture, irritable rather than tearful, with rumination on culpability. Shorter course; reconstitution faster, but documented.

**Episode 3 — Post-resurrection, current.** Most equivocal. Features muted by avoidance (see §2.2). Adjustment-level distress is inferable from behavioral data — increased self-deprecating humor density, deflection of intimate inquiry, accelerated return-to-function pace — even where vegetative signs are not on record. Provisional only.

**Course.** Episodic, stressor-tied, fully remitting between events. No chronicity. No baseline dysphoria.

### 2.2 Post-Traumatic Stress, Subthreshold, Avoidance-Predominant — current

**DSM-analog: V71.09 / "other specified trauma-and-stressor-related disorder," subthreshold PTSD.** Does **not** meet full PTSD criteria; the criteria it touches it touches incompletely.

**Criterion A (qualifying event).** Met emphatically: violent death by impalement at the hands of an Orchis assassin. Resurrection does not erase the antecedent experience; somatic memory of the event is presumptively encoded.

**Criterion B (intrusion).** Minimally documented. This is the central interpretive question: is this true absence, or under-reporting? The file's assessment is **under-reporting** — both narrative (the canon does not depict her interior with diagnostic granularity) and characterological (a subject whose dominant defense against the death is avoidance is, by definition, unlikely to report intrusions to anyone). Provisional: presumed present, low-to-moderate severity, contained.

**Criterion C (avoidance).** Met robustly. She does not discuss the death. She does not contextualize her resurrection in conversation. She returns to operational activity at an accelerated pace inconsistent with normal grief or trauma processing. Topic-aversion is observable in micro-behaviors: she switches subjects, jokes, redirects to others' concerns, leaves rooms.

**Criterion D (negative alterations in cognition/mood).** Partial. No global numbing; no anhedonia outside event-locked windows. Possible mild persistent negative belief about self ("I am the reason X was hurt") chronically present pre-resurrection regarding Bruno and Kamala's Law, exacerbated rather than created by death event.

**Criterion E (arousal/reactivity).** Largely absent on record. No hypervigilance beyond operationally appropriate baseline. Sleep disturbance is multi-determined and predates the index event.

**Net.** Two criteria solidly met, two partial, one minimal. **Subthreshold.** The clinical concern is not present-state severity but *trajectory*: avoidance-predominant trauma presentations are the ones that compound silently and surface years later under additive stressors. This is the diagnosis most worth monitoring.

### 2.3 Identity-Related Distress, Adolescent, Above Normative Load — historical, attenuating

Not a disorder. A **dimensional finding** worth coding because of its causal role in her power-onset presentation. The Terrigenesis event externalized an unconscious assimilation wish into a literal phenotypic morph (Carol Danvers' body). The five-issue arc of un-morphing into her own face is correctly read as the resolution of a developmental crisis around bicultural identity that was sub-acute prior to power-onset. Current status: largely resolved, sublimated into her operational identity. Not relapsing.

### 2.4 Bereavement, Complicated Features — historical, partially worked through

Reframed for the file: Bruno's hand injury and his departure to Wakanda constitute a relational loss with persistent guilt-cognition. Not Prolonged Grief Disorder (the relationship was not terminated and has been intermittently reconstituted), but a chronic low-grade grief signature is present and well-tolerated.

---

## 3. SUBCLINICAL FEATURES (dimensional, not diagnostic)

The following are *traits or patterns* present at intensities below diagnostic threshold but operationally salient:

- **Hyperthymic temperament features.** Baseline mood positively skewed, high energy, high engagement, low need for solitude. Distinguishable from hypomania by stability (not episodic), reactivity (responds to environment), and absence of impulsivity-cluster signs.
- **Over-responsibility cognitive style.** Tendency to assume causal authorship for outcomes structurally beyond her control. Reaches thresholds of cognitive distortion ("personalization") during stress episodes; remits between.
- **Externalizing-of-aggression vulnerability.** The Stormranger episode demonstrated that her aggressive impulses, normally well-integrated, can be readily projected into an external object that "carries" them. Suggests a discrete area of incomplete integration around violent capacity. Currently dormant; recurrence risk if she acquires another technology or relationship that offers a similar receptacle.
- **Idealization-then-disillusionment cycle with authority figures.** Carol Danvers prototype. Pattern: pre-loads admiration onto a figure pre-acquaintance, defers to them past her own better judgment, sustains real injury when they fail, then over-corrects toward wariness. Pattern modulation is in progress; not yet extinguished.
- **Difficulty receiving care.** Reflexively deflects, jokes, redirects. Pre-power origin; not produced by trauma.
- **Sleep debt as chronic.** Operationally significant; not a disorder in itself but a vulnerability multiplier for everything else.

---

## 4. ETIOLOGY (formulation)

A standard biopsychosocial frame:

**Biological.** Unremarkable pre-power. Post-Terrigenesis / post-mutant-reclassification: a polymorphic phenotype with built-in identity instability at the somatic level — injury *forces* a return to baseline form, meaning the body cannot maintain a disguise under stress. This is etiologically relevant: her physiology recapitulates her psychology's central tension (the temptation and impossibility of passing). Endocrine and neurodevelopmental trajectories appear within normal limits. No family psychiatric history is on record; the Khan family is notable for affective stability, anxiety being limited to Muneeba's situational worry-cluster (not pathological).

**Psychological.** The protective factor of unusual magnitude is the family-of-origin secure base. Yusuf functions as a near-textbook attuned attachment figure; Muneeba supplies the ambivalent-resistant element without crossing into invalidation; Aamir provides peer-adjacent sibling solidarity. This combination produces an interior working model of *love as reliable and the world as the problem*, which is the rare attachment configuration that generates outward-directed rather than inward-directed pathology under stress. Her wounds become activism rather than depression; her aggression seeks structural targets rather than self.

The countervailing wound is **bicultural invisibility** — being seen-but-not-known by the majority culture. This is the substrate the powers landed on. The compensatory pre-power apparatus (fan-fiction, Avengers idealization, the substituted-self of writing herself as Carol) prefigured the literal morph. Recovery from the morph is the prototype of all her subsequent recoveries: the return to her own face.

**Social.** Jersey City as ecological holding environment — diverse, locally textured, neighborhood-as-village. The mosque, the Circle Q, the Carrelli household, the high school all function as a redundant social fabric that catches her when individual relationships fail. Her later operational decisions (founding the Champions on consent, refusing predictive justice) are direct extrapolations of values absorbed from this fabric.

**Etiology of present features.** Adjustment reactions cluster at the intersection of *moral injury* and *betrayal by trusted authority*, not at the intersection of *personal danger* and *threat to self*. This is the diagnostic fingerprint: she does not develop symptoms when nearly killed; she develops symptoms when she discovers her work has been used to harm others or that a figure she trusted has acted against her values. The vulnerability is values-shaped, not threat-shaped.

---

## 5. COURSE OVER TIME

**Pre-power baseline (childhood–age 16).** Sub-acute identity distress, normative-plus, compensated by fan-fiction and family. No clinical contacts indicated. Functioning high.

**Terrigenesis and origin arc (age 16, ~five-issue interval).** Acute identity crisis externalized somatically. Resolves through behavioral choice (refusal of morph) and value articulation (the home-made costume). No residual.

**Early heroic operations (year 1–2).** Stable functioning with normative adolescent stressors plus operational risk. No clinical events.

**Civil War II and Karachi (year 2–3).** First adjustment episode. Full remission via family contact and ideological reconstitution.

**Champions period (year 3–4).** Integrative — operational and ideological reform. Mood and functioning above baseline. Acquisition of leadership identity, though under-claimed.

**Stormranger arc (year 4).** Discrete episode of externalized aggression via exogenous technology. Resolved by destruction of the suit and explicit re-integration. Not a recurrence vulnerability unless analogous receptacle reappears.

**Outlawed and Kamala's Law (year 4–5).** Second adjustment episode. Compounded by physical injury and identity-as-pretext distress. Remission slower than first episode but complete.

**Death and resurrection / mutant reclassification (year 5–present).** Third, atypical episode. Avoidance-predominant. The most concerning datum in the file: the speed of return-to-function is incompatible with full processing. Subclinical at present; chronic-risk profile.

**Trajectory inference.** Resilience is high and improving. Insight is increasing with age. The chronic risk is *additive*: should two or more of her established stressor categories converge (moral injury + family endangerment + authority-betrayal), the avoidant residue from the resurrection event may decompensate into a more frank presentation.

---

## 6. COMORBIDITY

None at primary level. Within the subthreshold and dimensional space:

- Adjustment reactions and subthreshold PTSD share substrate (stressor-tied, event-locked) and are best read as a single underlying stress-response architecture manifesting differently across stressor types.
- Sleep debt is operationally comorbid with every episode — a multiplier rather than a disorder.
- The over-responsibility cognitive style is comorbid with every adjustment episode and is part of the predisposing matrix.

No substance use comorbidity (lifetime abstainer, religiously and constitutionally). No eating disorder despite an adolescent disordered *relationship* with food (food as identity battleground); appetite remained intact, weight stable, no compensatory behaviors, no body-image distortion in the clinical sense — the only "body-image" issue is her ability to literally change her body, which is a separate problem class.

---

## 7. DIFFERENTIAL: WHAT SHE IS NOT, AND WHY

The subject superficially evokes a number of diagnoses on cursory reading. Each is excluded with reasons specific to the case, because *which disorders she lacks* is itself diagnostically informative — it constrains her risk profile and rules out interventions that would be wrong.

### 7.1 Not Major Depressive Disorder

Affective range remains broad across all observation windows. Anhedonia is event-locked and domain-specific (loses interest in costume work after Civil War II; does not lose interest globally). No neurovegetative cluster: appetite reduces transiently, never with the persistent pattern; sleep is disturbed by schedule and trauma not by early-morning awakening or hypersomnia of depressive type; psychomotor activity is preserved or elevated, never retarded. No worthlessness cognition outside guilt-of-specific-act type (categorically distinct from depressive global self-devaluation). No suicidal ideation, active or passive, on record. **Excluded.**

### 7.2 Not Bipolar Spectrum

No discrete elevated mood episodes meeting duration thresholds. Enthusiasm and excitement are reactive (fan encounters, mission successes), not autonomous. No reduced need for sleep with preserved energy (her sleep debt produces fatigue, as in normals). No grandiosity (the *opposite* — under-claims). No goal-directed activity surge beyond baseline. No impulsivity-cluster (no spending sprees, no hypersexuality, no high-risk decision pattern outside operationally justified risk). The hyperthymic *trait* should not be mistaken for hypomanic episodes. **Excluded.**

### 7.3 Not Borderline Personality Disorder

Highest false-positive risk on careless reading, given the plural identity and the intense relationships. Excluded on every criterion: identity is plural-and-integrated, *not* unstable — she holds her many components simultaneously rather than oscillating between them. Relationships are durable across years (Bruno, family, Nakia, Champions roster); no idealization-devaluation cycling at the relational level (cycling is reserved for *roles*, like the Carol hero-template, not for the people). No chronic emptiness; rather, chronic fullness. No self-harm. No suicidal gesture pattern. Abandonment fears absent — she handles departures (Bruno to Wakanda) with grief but without the characteristic frantic-effort signature. Affective instability is event-locked, not minute-to-minute. **Excluded firmly.**

### 7.4 Not Narcissistic Personality Disorder

Idealization runs *outward* (Carol, the Avengers), never toward the self. Chronic under-claiming. Declines leadership titles even when functionally leading. No grandiose self-concept; no entitlement; empathy is overdeveloped, not deficient; no exploitation pattern. The opposite signature, if anything: a vulnerability to *under*-claiming her real authority. **Excluded.**

### 7.5 Not Histrionic Personality

Expressiveness and theatricality are present but are stylistic-cultural rather than need-driven; attention-seeking as a *motive* is absent (she is repeatedly surprised by attention, not soliciting it). Relationships are not shallow. **Excluded.**

### 7.6 Not Dissociative Identity Disorder

The Stormranger episode is the diagnostic trap. It is a *discrete external prosthesis* with autonomous behavior, not an internal alter system. No host-and-alter architecture; no amnestic barriers between self-states; no switching phenomena outside the suit's operation; the suit was a separable object that she destroyed. Her plural identity is integrated multiplicity (Pakistani / American / Muslim / Inhuman-now-mutant / hero / daughter / sister), all simultaneously present and co-conscious. This is *the opposite* of DID, which is fragmented identity with dissociative barriers. **Excluded.**

### 7.7 Not Obsessive-Compulsive Disorder

Religious observance is values-driven, not anxiety-driven; she misses prayers without compensatory ritualization; she experiments with halal boundaries (the bacon curiosity) — incompatible with the rigidity of OCD scrupulosity. No ego-dystonic intrusive obsessions; no time-consuming compulsive behavior outside operational duty cycles. **Excluded.** Note: should be re-screened if guilt-cognition around Bruno or the death event develops a ritual-attenuation pattern, which it has not.

### 7.8 Not Generalized Anxiety Disorder

Worry is realistic and operationally calibrated. No free-floating chronic anxiety. Somatic anxiety signature (muscle tension, GI symptoms, restlessness as trait) absent. **Excluded.** Her mother Muneeba would be a more plausible candidate; the subject is not.

### 7.9 Not Social Anxiety Disorder

She codes-switches across audiences without performance distress, public-speaks under fire, mediates between hostile parties. Early adolescent self-consciousness (the BLT scene, the morph as wish to be the more socially legible body) is normatively-coded and was sub-clinical. **Excluded.**

### 7.10 Not Body Dysmorphic Disorder

The unconscious wish for a different body manifested *literally* in the morph, but the resolution of the origin arc was the deliberate rejection of that body in favor of her own. She does not now display preoccupation with imagined defects, mirror checking, camouflaging, or reassurance-seeking. The costume design choices are religious-cultural, not concealing. **Excluded.**

### 7.11 Not Anorexia / Bulimia / Disordered Eating

Food was an identity battleground (halal, peer pressure, family) but never a control-of-body battleground. Weight, intake, and compensatory behaviors are all in the normal range. Episodic skipping is schedule-driven, not restriction-driven. **Excluded.**

### 7.12 Not "Hero / Savior Syndrome"

The most important non-clinical differential. Her drive is *community-rooted and consent-respecting*, not self-glorifying or paternalistic. The entire Champions thesis is an explicit refutation of saviorism — heroism as collaborative, accountable, and consent-based, founded specifically in repudiation of Carol's *Civil War II* posture. Where she drifts toward savior posture (Outlawed-era over-extension), she notices, self-corrects, and re-articulates the principle. The risk is real but the pattern is *self-detecting*, which is the opposite of the disorder. **Excluded.**

### 7.13 Not Adjustment Disorder *Chronic Subtype*

Each adjustment episode remits. Cumulative load is increasing, but no episode has gone chronic. To be re-evaluated if the post-resurrection avoidance persists past a further calendar year without integration.

### 7.14 Not a Psychotic-Spectrum Disorder

No hallucinations of endogenous origin, no delusions, no formal thought disorder, no negative symptoms. The exogenous Stormranger influence and any Inhuman/mutant perceptual phenomena are correctly attributed to their external substrates. **Excluded firmly.**

### 7.15 Not a Substance-Related Disorder

Lifetime abstainer from alcohol and recreational drugs. Caffeine use is moderate. No medication-misuse pattern. **Exc


## Behavioral Atlas

# UATU DOSSIER — KAMALA KHAN / MS. MARVEL
## SECTION VI: BEHAVIORAL ATLAS

A longitudinal catalog of the subject's observable behaviors, motor signatures, verbal patterns, decision heuristics, and micro-tells, indexed by internal state and external condition. Drawn from approximately one decade of canonical observation (2013–present). Where a behavior is era-specific (pre-Terrigenesis, post–*Civil War II*, post-resurrection), the era is noted; where it is invariant across the record, it is marked **[stable trait]**.

---

### I. BASELINE / CALM STATE

**Postural baseline.** Subject carries herself slightly hunched at the shoulders when stationary — a residual adolescent posture that persists into her later teen years even as her competence escalates. She occupies less spatial volume than her actual body warrants, a habit predating powers and inverse to her power set (which is volumetric expansion). The contradiction is diagnostic: she is a girl whose biology makes her large and whose socialization makes her small, and her resting posture honors the socialization.

**Hand behaviors.** Constant low-grade kinesis. Phone in left hand more often than right (left-thumb scrolling dominant); right hand free for gesture, food, or notebook. When listening to a person she likes, she pulls a sleeve cuff over her right thumb and worries the fabric — a self-soothing micro-tic visible from *Ms. Marvel* vol. 3 onward and stable across runs. When listening to a person she does not trust, the hands go behind her back or into pockets, fingers curled.

**Facial defaults.** Eyebrow-forward expression at rest — a slight, perpetual "wait, what?" quality even when not surprised, which reads as openness and is a primary reason peers and adults consistently underestimate her tactical mind. Smiles asymmetrically, right corner first, the left following a half-second later when the smile is genuine, simultaneously when it is performed for adults.

**Speech, calm.** Rapid, polysyllabic, allusive — fandom-saturated reference density approximately three to five embedded citations per minute of relaxed conversation (Avengers lore, anime, video games, classic SF, occasionally Urdu poetry inherited from Yusuf). Vocal pitch sits in upper-middle register; rises sharply with enthusiasm; drops a full octave when she is being serious in a way she does not want to be challenged on — a register-shift her family and Bruno have learned to read but most adversaries have not.

**Code-switching.** Continuous and mostly unconscious. With Muneeba: more deferential cadence, "ammi," Urdu loan-words, shorter sentences. With Yusuf: warmer, slower, more Urdu, more silences allowed. With Aamir: sibling banter register, theological needling, the only context she swears comfortably (mild, "crap"-grade). With Bruno: fastest tempo, lowest editing, most interruption-tolerance — her unguarded register. With Carol (pre–CWII): hushed, formal, pre-rehearsed; (post–CWII): clipped, declarative, eye-contact held longer than comfort. With Zoe Zimmer: initially defensive-bright, evolves toward genuine warmth post–Zoe's coming-out arc. With strangers in costume: a half-octave pitched-down "hero voice" she does not realize she has adopted.

**Eating, calm.** Picks. Halal observance plus chronic time-poverty produces a snack-grazing pattern rather than meals. Default fuel sources: Circle Q convenience-store rotation, Bruno's father's gyros (her single most reliable hot meal), Muneeba's leftovers eaten standing at the refrigerator at 1 a.m. She separates components on the plate before eating, working from least- to most-preferred — a child's strategy retained into adolescence. **[stable trait]**

**Reading/screen behavior.** Reads in bed lying on her stomach, feet kicked up, phone or laptop propped on a pillow. Tabs are never closed; her browser is an archeological record of overlapping interests. Notebooks (multiple, always physical, fine-tip pen) for fan-fic drafts, costume sketches, school notes, and — post-Champions — operational planning that she draws as if it were fan-art (panel layouts, speech balloons), a tell that her cognitive substrate for tactics is narrative.

**Prayer/observance, calm baseline.** Salat performed irregularly but not abandoned; more reliable on Fridays and during Ramadan; private, never performative. She does not wear hijab outside the mosque (a deliberate choice, not a rejection); her costume hood functions as a partial substitute and she touches it before high-stakes action in a gesture that is half adjustment and half blessing. **[stable trait, post-power]**

---

### II. UNDER LOW-GRADE STRESS (SCHOOL, FAMILY FRICTION, SOCIAL EXPOSURE)

**Verbal acceleration.** Words-per-minute spike approximately 30%. Reference density doubles. Self-interrupts mid-sentence to pivot to a related thought, then loops back ("wait — okay, so — but anyway"). This is her primary tell that she is anxious and trying to think her way out in real time.

**Physical fidgets.** Sleeve-worrying intensifies. Pen-clicking if a pen is available. Bounces right heel when seated. Tucks hair behind right ear repeatedly even when it has not moved — a grooming-displacement gesture inherited from observation of Muneeba.

**Avoidance micro-behaviors.** Develops sudden interest in her phone when a conversation she does not want enters its second beat. Will fake-receive a text to exit. Disappears from family dinners by volunteering to clear plates — work as escape.

**Lying tells.** She lies badly and knows it. Voice rises a quarter-octave; she over-explains; she adds unnecessary specificity ("I was at the library, the second-floor one, near the periodicals"); she breaks eye contact upward and to the right. Yusuf reads her instantly; Muneeba reads her instantly and confronts; Bruno reads her instantly and waits. Adversaries with any read-on-people competence catch her immediately, which is why her undercover work is consistently rescued by improvisation rather than craft. **[stable trait]**

---

### III. ACUTE THREAT / COMBAT

**Pre-engagement.** A two-stage transformation. First: the touch to the hood/scarf described above. Second: a deep inhale through the nose, audible to anyone close — her version of bracing. Eyes narrow; the eyebrow-forward "wait, what?" expression vanishes and is replaced by a flat, focused gaze that surprises adversaries who have profiled her as the goofy teen.

**Opening move.** She talks first. Almost always. A quip, a callout, a one-liner — partly genuine personality, partly tactical (drawing fire to herself, away from civilians; locating the opponent's temperament; buying a beat to scan terrain). The quip is also a self-regulation tool: she has externalized her fear into performance before the first punch lands.

**Power deployment hierarchy, observed.**

1. *Embiggened fist* — first reflex, used to intercept incoming force or seize/restrain. Preferred because it is the move closest to a hug-or-shield rather than a strike.
2. *Elongation* — used for reach, rescue (snatching a civilian, catching a fall), and disarmament. She uses elongation more than she uses force; it is her signature.
3. *Giant form (full embiggening)* — reserved for "stand between" moments: civilians behind her, threat ahead. She becomes literally a wall. Diagnostic of her self-concept: she is a barrier, not a sword.
4. *Embiggened feet* — used to stabilize when she is at risk of being thrown or knocked from a height; rarely used offensively.
5. *Shrinking* — least-used, reserved for infiltration and for the rare moment she wants to hide. She dislikes shrinking; it activates the invisibility wound.
6. *Shape mimicry* — used reluctantly and almost always poorly; her face when impersonating someone else is uncannily uncomfortable, an authorial choice that doubles as character truth.

**Strike economy.** She does not throw combinations. One large committed action, reassess, another. Trained fighters notice this — she is a brawler with a soft heart, not a martial artist. She has improved over the run but the underlying rhythm persists.

**Defensive habit.** She takes hits she should dodge. The healing-via-reversion mechanic has trained her to absorb damage rather than evade it; she trusts her body to reset and uses her form as a sponge for damage that would otherwise reach civilians or teammates. Long-term cost: chronic micro-traumas, sleep disruption, and an under-developed evasion skillset. **[stable trait, escalating concern]**

**Voice in combat.** Drops the upper-register chirp; settles into the half-octave-lower "hero voice." Quips persist but become shorter, more rhythmic. Profanity remains absent; her hardest cursing in combat is "oh come ON."

**Eye behavior in combat.** Tracks civilians first, threat second. This is reversed from professional combatants and is one of the most reliable behavioral signatures distinguishing her from impostors, shapeshifters, or clones (relevant: the Doc.X / Kamala Korps arc, where genuine Kamala was distinguishable by the involuntary civilian-first scan).

**Withdrawal/retreat.** She does not retreat under threat to herself; she retreats under threat to others she cannot protect from her current position. Her retreats are tactical relocations to better defend, not flights. The one canonical exception is post–*Civil War II* (Karachi), which was a moral retreat, not a tactical one — diagnostic of the kind of injury required to make her actually leave.

---

### IV. INTIMACY / TRUSTED COMPANY

**With Bruno specifically.** Sits closer than she sits to anyone else. Steals from his plate without asking — a behavior she does not perform with anyone else, including family. Finishes his sentences when excited; lets him finish hers when tired. Touch is frequent but de-eroticized — shoulder bumps, sleeve-tugs, the occasional brief hand-on-arm — and she has, throughout the run, conspicuously failed to interrogate why this register is so comfortable to her. Post–Bruno's injury and departure to Wakanda: the comfort behaviors persist on his return but with a hesitation-beat before each, a half-second of permission-checking she did not previously require.

**With Yusuf.** Tucks her head into his shoulder when sad — the single most reliable indicator that she is past her own coping capacity. Receives his counsel without rebuttal, a deference she extends to no one else. Reads Urdu poetry with him aloud, mispronouncing without embarrassment, which is itself a tell of how safe she feels with him.

**With Muneeba.** Argues. The arguing is the love. Quieter when they are not arguing — a chilly détente means something is wrong. Post–Muneeba's discovery of the secret identity, she lets her mother fuss without resistance, accepts food without protest, a behavioral marker of relief that the central lie is gone.

**With Aamir.** Sibling needling that masks the deepest sibling bond in the file. Teases his devoutness, defends it ferociously to outsiders. Touches her brother's shoulder when she leaves a room — a small benediction she does not perform with others.

**With the Champions.** Adopts a posture she does not adopt elsewhere: shoulders back, chin up, the spatial-occupation she suppresses in civilian life permitted because she is responsible *for* them. The team is the one social context where she allows herself to be seen at her actual size, metaphorically and sometimes literally.

**Receiving care.** Pathologically awkward. Compliments produce a head-duck, a hand-to-back-of-neck gesture, and an immediate self-deprecating deflection ("oh, no, I'm — anyway"). Gifts are received with elaborate gratitude that exceeds the gift, a tell of how little she expects to be given to. Physical affection from non-family is received with a freeze-then-melt pattern — a half-second of stillness before reciprocation.

---

### V. GRIEF

**Acute grief, fresh.** Goes quiet. The voluble verbal style collapses inward; she becomes monosyllabic, which is the most reliable grief-signature in the file because it is so out of band. Stops eating in a way she does not stop eating under any other stressor.

**Mid-term grief.** Over-functions. Cleans her room, reorganizes her notebooks, takes on extra patrols, helps Muneeba in the kitchen without being asked. Grief expressed through productive motion. **[stable trait, post–*Civil War II* and post-Bruno's injury and post-resurrection]**

**Long-term grief.** Sublimates into policy. The Champions are a grief-object — a structural response to what Carol did. Kamala's Law era: she organized her grief about her own near-death into protectiveness of younger heroes. This is her highest-functioning grief expression and also her most dangerous, because it converts unprocessed wound into long-term mission and forecloses interior reckoning.

**Avoidance signature, post-resurrection.** Will not discuss the death. Changes subject with a humor-pivot ("anyway, dying is overrated, ten out of ten do not recommend, moving on"). Sleeps less; patrols more; jokes more frequently and less well. The jokes are shorter and land softer — a diagnostic micro-tell that the comedy is now defensive rather than expressive.

**Tears.** Private. Almost exclusively in bedroom or bathroom, doors closed. Public tears occur only twice in the canonical record under conditions of moral injury rather than personal loss — diagnostic that her grief about her *values* is the grief she cannot contain.

---

### VI. VICTORY

**Immediate post-victory.** Whoops. Genuine, unguarded, often arms-up. Lasts approximately four to six seconds before the self-monitoring resumes and she pivots to checking on others ("everyone okay? everyone okay?"). The whoop is one of the most reliable Kamala-authentic markers in the file — clones and impostors consistently fail to produce it with the right unselfconscious volume.

**Credit-handling.** Deflects. "It was a team thing." "Honestly Bruno did the math." "I just hit it." Refuses interviews when possible; when unavoidable, gives credit to Jersey City as an entity, a rhetorical move that has become her signature. **[stable trait]**

**Private celebration.** Texts Bruno. Eats. Sleeps deeply for the first time in days — sleep-debt repayment is her body's victory ritual.

**Public celebration.** Uncomfortable. Awards and recognitions trigger the back-of-neck gesture, the asymmetric performed smile, and the rapid-pivot-to-anecdote-about-someone-else.

---

### VII. DEFEAT / FAILURE

**Tactical defeat (lost the fight, no civilian casualties).** Frustration expressed as kinetic — pacing, embiggened fist into a wall (apologized to), rapid verbal post-mortem at high speed. Recovers within hours via planning the next attempt.

**Moral defeat (won the fight but at unacceptable cost).** This is her break-state. Goes still. Voice drops out entirely. Withdrawal sequence initiates: first to bedroom, then to disengagement from team, then — at the deepest gradient — to geographic flight (Karachi precedent). Recovery requires not victory but *re-articulation of principle* — she comes back online when she can name what went wrong and what she will do differently, often by founding or reforming an institution.

**Failure to protect a specific person.** Self-punishing. Bruno's hand is the paradigm. Behaviors observed: increased patrol hours, decreased sleep, decreased eating, increased apologizing for unrelated minor things (displacement), and a particular flinch when the injured party enters the room — a half-second eye-break she does not perform with anyone else.

**Being deceived by a trusted figure.** Carol-template. Slow to update, then updates catastrophically — once trust breaks she does not partially reinstate it. The post–CWII Carol relationship is the canonical record: cordial, never again unguarded, a permanent half-step of distance she does not herself recognize she is maintaining.

---

### VIII. DECISION HEURISTICS

**Heuristic 1: "What would a hero do?"** Primary decision frame, especially pre–CWII. Adaptive in providing a stable ethical compass; maladaptive when the heroes she modeled on are themselves wrong. She has, post–CWII, partially upgraded this to "what would a hero *who learned from Carol's mistake* do?" — a generational reform built into her decision substrate.

**Heuristic 2: Consent-first.** Will not coerce. Will not surveil. Will not detain without due process. This is her most stable post–CWII principle and operates as a near-absolute deontological constraint. Cost-tolerant; she will accept tactical loss to preserve it.

**Heuristic 3: Civilians first, teammates second, self last.** Her triage order in every documented engagement. The "self last" rule is the source of most of her medical events.

**Heuristic 4: Institutions get less benefit of the doubt than individuals.** Acquired through experience. Will trust a stranger before she trusts a stranger's employer. Notable in her dealings with SHIELD, the legal apparatus around Kamala's Law, and Orchis-adjacent entities.

**Heuristic 5: When in doubt, talk first.** Defaults to negotiation, even with figures most heroes would engage kinetically. Has been wrong about this twice in the record and right far more often.

**Heuristic 6: When morally cornered, withdraw and re-articulate.** Her break-glass response. She does not escalate against others; she escalates against her own current configuration and rebuilds.

**Heuristic 7: Family is non-negotiable.** The one heuristic that overrides all others, including consent-first. Threats to Yusuf, Muneeba, or Aamir produce a Kamala who is operationally unlike her baseline self: faster, harder, less verbal, willing to use force she would otherwise refuse. Adversaries who have triggered this state have universally regretted it.

---

### IX. DAILY / WEEKLY ROUTINES (RECONSTRUCTED PATTERN-OF-LIFE)

**Weekday morning.** Late riser, chronically. Alarm at 6:45, actual rise 7:10, twenty-minute scramble to school. Breakfast skipped or chai-and-toast at the door. Phone check before feet hit floor. **[stable trait]**
