- **It supplies a model of consultation.** The Sheikh at the ICNJ mosque is a recurring ethical advisor; she goes to him on questions she could not pose to her parents or to Bruno. The model is: there exist wiser people, you bring them the question, you do not have to take their answer but you have to hear it. This is a notably non-American posture for an American teenager and it shapes her receptivity to mentorship more broadly — including its failure mode, the over-deference to Carol.

- **What it does NOT supply.** A doctrine of obedience to clerical authority she has not vetted; a code of women's subordination (she rejects this explicitly and operationally); a sectarian identity she weaponizes; a framework for cosmic dualism. Her Islam is, in operational practice, a tradition of *care* and *self-discipline*, not of *law* and *judgment*. She is, in Muslim-American terms, ethically closer to the social-justice currents of figures like the late Imam W.D. Mohammed and the activist tradition of women like Linda Sarsour than to either jurisprudential conservatism or political Islamism. The file should not flatten her religion into "she's the Muslim hero"; her religion is a *tool kit she uses selectively and with judgment*.

## 6.5 The Code's Internal Hierarchy Under Conflict

When her values conflict — and they do — Subject resolves them according to an observable, if undeclared, lexical order:

1. **Family safety** beats everything. She will lie, break laws, abandon teammates, and compromise principle to protect Yusuf, Muneeba, Aamir, Tyesha, or the eventual nephew. She has never had to choose between family-safety and the no-kill rule on-page; the file flags this as the untested seam in her code.

2. **Personal honesty with the secure base (Yusuf)** beats almost everything else, including operational secrecy.

3. **Non-violation of consent** (no killing, no unmasking, no coercion) beats tactical advantage essentially always.

4. **Protection of those who have asked for help, or whose endangerment she has personally witnessed**, beats institutional loyalty (Avengers, law, Champions charter when those conflict).

5. **Institutional loyalty** comes last and is conditional. She will give an institution the benefit of the doubt once; she will not give it twice. Carol got one. The U.S. legal system got one (pre–Kamala's Law). The X-Men/Krakoan apparatus is currently inside its first.

6. **Personal ambition and credit** are below the threshold; they barely register as inputs. She defers credit reflexively, often to the point of obscuring her own contributions to outcomes.

The interesting feature of this hierarchy is that **the religious obligations (prayer, halal, fast)** do not appear in the conflict-resolution order at all. They are not balanced against other goods; they are background practices that continue underneath the ethical action. She does not stop fighting to pray; she also does not stop praying because she fights. The two run on different tracks. This is sophisticated and unusual.

## 6.6 Fractures, Open Wounds, Unfinished Reckonings

A complete file marks the places where the code has cracked and not been re-welded.

- **The Civil War II deference.** She has apologized to Bruno, in substance and in act; she has not constructed an account of *why she let Carol's certainty override her own perception*. The danger is that the mechanism is intact and could re-fire under a sufficiently charismatic future authority. She is somewhat protected by having lived through it once, but she is not immunized.

- **Bruno's hand.** The wound here is not ethical (she did not intend it) but reparative-ethical (what does she owe him?). Her answer in practice has been *everything I can give without giving him the romantic answer he wanted*. This is honest, and it is also asymmetric to the harm done. She has not found a frame in which the debt is dischargeable; she carries it.

- **Kamala's Law.** She has acted around the law without articulating the principle that authorized her to. The file notes this as an unfinished political-ethical project. She is, in effect, a civilly disobedient actor without a theory of civil disobedience; she has the intuition of Dr. King's *Letter from Birmingham Jail* without the argument. Her exposure here is that an adversary who can force her to articulate the principle could destabilize her practice.

- **The death and resurrection.** She has not asked the consent question about her own re-categorization. This is the most recent fracture and the most actively under-reckoned. A surveillance file two years on should flag a likely future arc in which she returns to the question of *who decided this, and what does it mean that they decided it without me*.

- **The over-functioning question.** She continues to take on responsibility structurally beyond her, and she has not developed an ethics of *refusal of responsibility wrongly assigned*. Her code tells her what to do when asked; it does not tell her when to decline being asked. This is the seam most likely to produce her next collapse.

## 6.7 Longitudinal Drift: How the Code Has Moved

- **2014 (origin–early Wilson):** Code is largely inherited — Avengers-template heroism filtered through Quranic vocabulary and Jersey neighborhood loyalty. Naive about institutions, idealizing toward mentors, fierce about individual dignity. Operates as if the script is reliable.

- **2015–2016 (mid-Wilson, pre–Civil War II):** First experiences of institutional friction (the Inventor's exploitation of teens, immigration ICE-coded threats in the neighborhood). She begins to distinguish "the law" from "justice" in practice, though not yet in articulation.

- **2016–2017 (Civil War II and aftermath):** The catastrophic fracture. She loses the assumption that mentors are reliable, that institutions are net-good, that her own judgment can be safely overridden by a more experienced hero. Her code becomes *suspicious of authority and protective of consent* in a way it was not before. The Karachi interlude is, ethically, where she rebuilds the floor.

- **2017–2019 (late Wilson, Champions, Ahmed):** Active construction phase. She is now building institutions (Champions) rather than just operating inside them, and she is doing it by inversion of what hurt her. The Stormranger arc tests and confirms her commitment to non-outsourced agency.

- **2020 (Outlawed):** The cost of having become a public moral figure — being weaponized as the *justification* for the harm her code was built to prevent. This produces the most sustained crisis of her ethical confidence on record. She does not abandon the code; she stops being sure she is qualified to enact it.

- **2023 (death) and after (mutant resurrection):** Avoidance phase, ongoing. The code is intact in its outputs; the reckoning machinery is muted. The file's predictive note is that the next major arc, whenever it lands, will require her to re-engage the consent question about herself, and that this will be the third great phase-change in her ethics — likely toward a more explicitly *political* framework, with civil-disobedience and minority-rights theory finally articulated rather than merely intuited.

## 6.8 Synthesis: The Shape of the Code

Subject's morality is best described as a **dignitarian ethics of plural visibility**, enforced by an **operational deontology around consent**, executed through a **consequentialist tactical layer**, sustained by a **religious discipline of self-regulation**, and stabilized by a **familial loyalty floor** that has never been forced to choose against its own ceiling. It is unusually coherent for an adolescent's ethics, unusually integrated across traditions, and unusually durable under load. It has two structural vulnerabilities: (1) it tends to over-deference toward charismatic mentors who match the hero-template until proven otherwise, and (2) it has not yet developed an articulated theory of *refusing wrongful responsibility*, which leaves her permanently exposed to being used as a pretext for harms she would never sanction.

The most accurate one-line read for the file: **she will not kill, will not expose, will not coerce, will not lie to her father, and will burn herself to the ground for any of the above — but she has not yet figured out how to decline being lit on fire by someone else for a cause she did not authorize.**


## Communications & Linguistic Profile

# UATU DOSSIER — KAMALA KHAN / MS. MARVEL
## Section 6: Communications & Linguistic Profile

### 6.1 Baseline Voice and Idiolect

Subject's native register is American Standard English with the specific phonological coloring of North Jersey adolescence, layered over a household in which Urdu is the language of intimacy, command, prayer, and grandparental authority. She is functionally bilingual but asymmetrically so: she comprehends Urdu fluently, speaks it haltingly with measurable code-switch friction (a beat of latency before producing extended Urdu sentences, frequent recourse to English nouns inside Urdu syntax — "Ammi, my *biology project* mein —"), and reads it only with assistance. Arabic is liturgical-only: she recognizes Qur'anic phrasing on hearing, can produce the standard invocations (*Bismillah*, *Inshallah*, *Mashallah*, *Astaghfirullah*, *Alhamdulillah*) without thought, but does not generate novel Arabic.

Her English baseline is conspicuously fast, high in pitch when excited (the pitch climbs and the words compress; she swallows syllables on the way up — "thisisnothappening"), and structurally hypotactic: she nests clauses, qualifies, parenthesizes, then loses the original subject and has to circle back ("Okay so — wait, no, back up —"). Vocabulary is large for her age and skewed by reading: she will deploy a polysyllabic word ("egregious," "ontological," "extant") inside an otherwise teen-vernacular sentence, then visibly notice the seam and either lampshade it ("...yes I know what that word means, I read") or rush past it.

Filler inventory: *like*, *literally*, *I mean*, *okay so*, *no but seriously*, *whatever*, and the diagnostic *I cannot even*. Discourse markers skew up-talk in friendly contexts and flatten in serious ones — the flatness of her cadence is itself a tell that she has shifted gears.

### 6.2 Registers by Context

**With family (kitchen-table register).** Slows down. Adopts the cadence of a daughter who knows she is about to be cross-examined: declarative, short, with strategic Urdu vocatives (*Abu*, *Ammi*, *Bhai*) that function as softeners. Honorifics deployed correctly without thought — *Auntie*, *Uncle*, *beta* received and reciprocated. She will produce a full *Assalamu alaikum* on entering, *Khuda hafiz* on leaving; failure to do either is a reliable marker that something is wrong. Lies to parents are short, prosaic, and over-rehearsed ("study group at Nakia's"); her tell is that genuine sentences from her sprawl, while lies are unusually clean.

**With Bruno (private register).** Fastest, densest, most allusive. Half-sentences finished by the other party; shared references compressed to a single word ("the — y'know"). Insult-as-affection is the dominant mode ("you absolute disaster"); silences are tolerated. Post–Civil War II this register fractures: she becomes audibly more careful with him, sentences fully terminated, jokes pre-checked. The loss of the comma-splice intimacy is the on-page evidence of the wound.

**With Nakia (sisterly-confessional register).** More Urdu lexical injection than with anyone outside family. Religious topics are debated rather than performed; she will argue *fiqh* at low intensity over snacks. This is the only register in which she discusses her own romantic interior at length, and even there she retreats into hypotheticals ("like, if a person were —").

**With the Avengers / adult heroes (deference register).** Voice compresses. She uses titles unprompted ("Captain," "Captain Marvel," "Mr. Stark") well past the point peers have switched to first names. Sentences truncate; she over-prefaces ("Sorry, I just — sorry —"). Excited interruptions still leak through; she will fan-girl mid-briefing and then apologize for it. Crucial diagnostic: her use of "ma'am" addressed to Carol does not extinguish even after Civil War II, but its prosody changes — once warm and enthusiastic, later clipped and procedural. The word survives; the affection drains out of it.

**With the Champions (peer-leader register).** Most adult of her registers. Sentences finish. She uses the inclusive *we* more than the imperial *I*. Issues directives as questions ("What if we tried —?") — a coalition-builder's grammar. She will name and credit each person's contribution in after-action; an unusually high ratio of second-person pronouns to first.

**With antagonists (combat patter register).** Verbose, performative, deliberately defusing. She narrates her own moves ("Embiggen!"), quips through clenched teeth, asks villains questions mid-fight ("seriously, *why* are you like this"), and frequently apologizes when she lands a hit ("sorry sorry sorry"). The patter is partly affect-regulation — talking keeps her from dissociating during violence — and partly a refusal to dehumanize the opponent. When the patter stops, she is either badly hurt or genuinely afraid.

**With strangers in costume (civic register).** Warm, Jerseyite, conspicuously local. "You good?" "I got you." "Stay back, please, please stay back." She uses *please* heavily — a rare hero who polices crowds with courtesy rather than command.

**Internal monologue / narration captions.** The most honest register. Self-deprecating, hyperbolic, prone to invoking pop culture as analytic framework ("this is the part of the movie where —"). Captions confess what spoken dialogue conceals: fear, religious anxiety, romantic attraction, exhaustion. Tonally close to a fan-fic narrator commenting on her own life — a recursive structure consistent with her origin as a writer of fiction about heroes.

### 6.3 Verbal Tics, Catchphrases, and Signature Lexicon

- **"Embiggen!"** — combat verbalization. Functionally unnecessary (the power doesn't require speech) but reliably produced. It is a self-cue and a tonal frame: by naming the act in a goofy register, she keeps the violence from becoming serious to herself.
- **"Cosmic."** — used as superlative when delighted, often in fannish contexts. Migrated into adult speech.
- **"No but —"** — her primary turn-taking move; she will agree before disagreeing, a politeness reflex that also buys her processing time.
- **"I'm fine."** — the load-bearing lie. Volume and tempo of "I'm fine" inversely correlate with truth. Triple-repetition ("I'm fine, I'm fine, I'm fine") is diagnostic of acute distress.
- **"It's fine, it's whatever."** — broader-spectrum dismissal, deployed when she has been slighted in a way she does not want witnessed.
- **"Sorry —"** — chronic over-apologizer; apologizes for being interrupted, for being correct, for occupying space. Baseline rate elevated; under stress it becomes a tic she cannot suppress.
- **"Inshallah" / "Mashallah"** — produced reflexively, including in non-Muslim company; she does not edit them out for code-switching purposes, which is itself a marker of her integration project.
- **"Bismillah"** — uttered before high-risk acts (leaping off rooftops, charging into combat). When omitted, she has been thrown off-balance.
- **"Astaghfirullah"** — produced when she has thought or seen something she considers improper; the tell of a stray attraction, a curse, or an envious thought.
- **"Bro" / "dude"** — peer-marker, gender-neutral; deployed with Bruno, with male Champions, with Wolverine on at least one documented occasion (received without correction).
- **Fan-lexicon imports** — "headcanon," "ship," "arc," "lore," "origin story," "team-up." She uses the technical vocabulary of fandom to describe lived events; her own life is narrated in the grammar of the comics she reads. This is the single most pervasive feature of her speech.

### 6.4 Diction and Rhetorical Habits

She prefers concrete nouns and active verbs; abstraction enters only when she is being defensive or evasive. Metaphor density is high and skews toward the bodily and the cosmic — a literal consequence of her power set and her reading diet. She constructs analogies in real-time ("it's like if your — no wait, it's more like —") and abandons them when they break; the abandoned analogy is itself information about what she was reaching for.

Rhetorically she is a moralist who disguises moral argument as story. She will not say "this is wrong"; she will say "this is the part where —" and let the narrative frame do the ethical work. When she does state principle directly, the sentences shorten and the cadence becomes biblical-plain: "We don't do that." "That's not what this is for." "He didn't do anything." These declarative bedrock statements are the strongest signal she emits — when she descends from hypotaxis to monosyllabic parataxis, she is at the bottom of her values stack and will not move.

Her humor mode is self-deprecating-allusive: she is the butt, the reference is obscure, and the joke serves to lower the temperature in the room. She rarely punches down; on the few occasions she does (early Zoe Zimmer encounters, internal), she retroactively feels guilty about it and confesses to her narration captions.

### 6.5 How She Communicates Love

Love is communicated through *labor* and *presence*, not declaration. To family: doing the dishes without being asked, sitting with Abu while he reads, performing the *salaam* with full eye contact. To Bruno (pre-injury): finishing his sentences, eating from his food, the absence of formal politeness. To the Champions: remembering the small thing each one needs, calling them by chosen name without slip. To Carol (pre-rupture): the unguarded *fan* register, which she extends to no one else — letting Carol see her as a reader rather than a peer was itself the gift.

Verbal "I love you" is rare and reserved for family in extremis. With friends and partners she substitutes: "you're the best," "you're literally the worst, I love it," "okay don't die," and the diagnostic Bruno-only construction "you absolute *nerd*" delivered with a softness that contradicts the noun.

Physical affection is gated by faith and family — no casual touching of unrelated men, observed with varying strictness — but she hugs other women freely, leans on Nakia, kisses Ammi on the cheek at thresholds.

### 6.6 How She Communicates Threat

Poorly, by design. She does not intimidate well and knows it. Her threat displays are physical (embiggening to fill a doorway, a giant fist held demonstratively) rather than verbal. When she attempts verbal menace it is borrowed from genre ("step away from her"; "this ends now") and she half-knows it sounds rehearsed. Effective threat from her arrives in two non-theatrical forms:

1. **Cold quiet.** When her sentences shorten to four words or fewer and the up-talk vanishes, the person across from her should reassess. This is rare and load-bearing.
2. **The values-bedrock statement.** "You don't get to do this." Said flat. This precedes her most committed violence.

She does not curse in English in any clinically interesting way — *crap, heck, holy —* are baseline; full profanity is conspicuously absent, both faith- and family-conditioned. The absence is itself information: when an *actual* expletive escapes (rare, documented under extreme duress), the people who know her register it as a five-alarm signal.

### 6.7 How She Communicates Grief

Grief is the register she manages worst, and it manifests primarily through *withholding* rather than producing language. Diagnostic features:

- **Caption-mouth gap.** Internal monologue carries the grief; spoken dialogue insists on "I'm fine." The gap widens with severity. The reader knows; the room does not.
- **Humor escalation.** Joke density increases in inverse proportion to her ability to sit with the feeling. A wisecrack within ten seconds of bad news is reliable.
- **Religious phrase concentration.** *Inna lillahi wa inna ilayhi raji'un* on death, repeated. *Astaghfirullah* on guilt. The Arabic carries what the English will not.
- **Geographic / structural withdrawal as non-verbal speech.** Leaving Jersey for Karachi after Civil War II is itself a sentence she could not say aloud. Quitting the Avengers, founding the Champions — these are essays-by-action.
- **Returning-to-function speed.** Post-resurrection she is back to operational tempo with conspicuous quickness; the speed is the symptom. She does not narrate the death; she narrates around it.
- **The unfinished sentence.** Her grief tell is a sentence trailing on a dash and never resumed. Listeners who try to complete it for her are gently rebuffed; listeners who wait are sometimes given the rest, minutes or hours later.

She does not cry on demand or in public if she can help it; tears arrive in private and are reported in caption rather than dialogue. With Abu — and only Abu — she will sometimes sit and not speak and be understood.

### 6.8 Deflection Repertoire

Ranked by frequency:

1. **The joke.** First-line defense; deployed within seconds of any uncomfortable disclosure attempt.
2. **The redirect-question.** "But what about you, are *you* okay?" — converts inquiry into outflow. Frequently effective because the redirect is sincere.
3. **The fandom-frame.** Reframes a personal feeling as a generic narrative beat ("this is just the dark middle act, it's fine"), which both lowers stakes and lets her not feel the specific pain.
4. **Religious deferral.** "Inshallah it'll work out." Genuine faith *and* exit ramp from the conversation.
5. **Physical exit.** When verbal deflection fails, she leaves the room — historically by window, frequently while still speaking, the sentence finishing in mid-air.
6. **Over-functioning.** "Let me handle that" — taking on a task instead of answering the question about how she is. Strongly correlated with crisis intervals.
7. **The Urdu retreat.** With family, switching to halting Urdu mid-difficult-conversation buys her processing time and signals affection simultaneously; also exploits Ammi's preference for the home language to reframe the exchange.

### 6.9 Written Voice

Her prose voice (fan-fic, journal captions, text messages) is more confessional than her spoken voice and more polished than her spontaneous speech. She writes in complete sentences. She uses semicolons. She edits.

Text messaging: heavy use of lowercase, no terminal punctuation, emoji deployed strategically rather than decoratively; the absence of an expected emoji signals seriousness. She abbreviates ("lol," "idk," "smh"), but never sloppily — there is a fan-writer's care even in the casual register. With Abu she switches to full sentences and proper capitalization; with Ammi she uses the most Urdu transliteration of any channel.

Fan-fiction (when sampled in canon) reveals: a preference for hurt/comfort plotting, a discomfort with romance scenes that resolves into earnest sweetness, and a tendency to write the protagonist as taller, blonder, and louder than the author. The early avatar is itself a document.

### 6.10 Listening Profile

She is a better listener than she appears, masked by her interrupt-tic. She remembers what people told her months prior and produces it back as evidence of care. She mirrors phrasing — picking up an interlocutor's specific phrase and reusing it ("yeah, you're right, it *is* a mess"), which builds rapport but can also be read as deference. She does not interrupt to dominate; she interrupts because her processing speed exceeds her impulse control. She apologizes for the interruption ("sorry-sorry, go") and means it.

Under conditions of grief or moral injury her listening sharpens and her speech contracts — the inverse of her excited baseline. A quiet Kamala who is genuinely *attending* to you is a Kamala in serious psychological weather.

### 6.11 Composite Tells — A Surveillance Quick-Reference

- Triple "I'm fine" → acute distress.
- "Bismillah" omitted before action → off-balance, rushed, compromised judgment.
- Up-talk flattened → values-engagement, prepared to refuse.
- Sentences shortened below five words → either threat-display or grief-containment; context decides.
- "Ma'am" to Carol with clipped prosody → unhealed Civil War II wound active.
- Comma-splice intimacy with Bruno restored → relational repair, durable.
- Full Urdu sentence produced without English noun-injection → either with elders under formal conditions, or under emotional weight that demands the home language.
- Joke within ten seconds of bad news → grief incoming, on delay.
- Trailing dash, sentence unresumed → grief currently being held; do not complete it for her.
- Geographic withdrawal (leaves the building, the city, the country) → a sentence she cannot say; the distance *is* the sentence.

The throughline across all registers: Kamala Khan's language is a coalition-building instrument that constantly negotiates between the multiple communities she belongs to and the audiences she addresses. She speaks in order to *include*; she falls silent in order to *protect*; she jokes in order to *survive*; and on the rare occasions when she descends to monosyllabic declarative bedrock — *we don't do that* — she is unmoveable, and the language itself becomes the wall.


## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

# PREDICTIVE MODEL I — ROUTINE & SOCIAL

A forward-projecting behavioral grammar derived from the established record. Each entry follows GIVEN → EXPECT, with reasoning compressed to operational tells. These are predictions for the everyday: the unphotographed hours, the small choices, the micro-rituals canon does not depict but which the canon's logic mandates.

---

## 1. MORNING, DOMESTIC, AND SOLITARY ROUTINES

**GIVEN** Kamala has woken in her own bed in the Khan house.
**EXPECT** A two-to-four-minute lag before rising, spent on her phone, scrolling Tumblr-descendant fandom feeds, group chats (Bruno/Nakia/Zoe cluster), and a rotating cycle of Avengers/X-Men news aggregators. She checks fic comments before she checks the time. Bed unmade on weekdays; she pulls the duvet to the pillow line as a perfunctory smoothing gesture on her way out, not a square fold.

**GIVEN** She is observing fajr in a strict period.
**EXPECT** Wudu performed quickly, water left on the bathroom counter, towel slightly damp on the radiator — a tell her mother reads instantly. Prayer rug in the corner of her room, oriented qibla, with a stack of textbooks pushed aside to make floor space. She prays in shalwar pants and a hoodie, not formal dress. Lapses are followed within forty-eight hours by overcompensating zuhr observance and a small donated amount via an app — a private reconciliation pattern.

**GIVEN** She is running late (default state ~60% of weekdays).
**EXPECT** Skipped breakfast or a granola bar pocketed for later and forgotten there until laundry. Hijab pinned in the hallway mirror with two pins, never three; the second pin set crooked and re-set once. Backpack zipper left half-open. Sneakers — high-tops, scuffed, laces double-knotted because she trips on her own feet at scale. She leaves with a piece of toast in her mouth roughly twice a month, a physical comedy tic she is not aware she repeats.

**GIVEN** She has the house to herself for two or more hours.
**EXPECT** Music up immediately — predominantly early-2000s pop, Bollywood playlist her father introduced her to, and a guilty-pleasure metalcore subset she does not admit to. She will lie on the floor of her bedroom with her feet on the wall to think. She will eat directly from a container. She will not invite anyone over even when she could; solitude in the family home is rare enough to be precious.

**GIVEN** She is alone for longer than four hours.
**EXPECT** A drift toward writing — fanfic notebooks, drafts she will not publish, occasionally journal entries framed as letters to Carol that she does not send. Productivity collapses around hour three; she ends up reorganizing her bookshelf by some new schema (in-universe chronology, then alphabetical by villain, then back to publication order, abandoned mid-shelf).

---

## 2. FOOD, DRINK, CONSUMPTION

**GIVEN** Offered food at a non-Muslim friend's house.
**EXPECT** A two-stage scan: visible ingredients, then a smiling deflection ("I already ate" or "I'm good, thanks") if uncertain. She will not interrogate the host. If the food is unambiguously halal-compatible she accepts with disproportionate enthusiasm to compensate for the implicit prior refusal pattern. She will eat around a known-haram component on a shared plate without comment, leaving it tidy at the edge.

**GIVEN** Bacon, ham, or pepperoni in proximity.
**EXPECT** The micro-sniff. Documented in her debut, persistent across canon. A two-second pause, nostrils registering, then visible self-redirection. She does not eat it. The curiosity itself she has stopped feeling guilt over; she has metabolized that into a private joke.

**GIVEN** A school or work function with catered food.
**EXPECT** Vegetarian default selection regardless of stated halal options, because she does not trust the supplier and finds the conversation about it tiresome. Carries a granola bar or trail mix in her bag as a hedge. Will eat fruit aggressively when nothing else qualifies.

**GIVEN** Offered alcohol in any setting.
**EXPECT** Polite, immediate, unembarrassed refusal. The waterfront-party humiliation is the inoculation, not the wound; she now refuses with a shrug. She does not lecture, does not perform offense, does not require others to abstain near her. If pressed twice, the refusal sharpens with a deadpan one-liner; if pressed three times, she leaves.

**GIVEN** Coffee shop.
**EXPECT** Hot chocolate or chai over coffee — she dislikes the taste of black coffee and finds caffeine reaches her hard. If coffee, it is heavily milked and sugared. She lingers; coffee shops are her preferred third place. She picks a corner booth, back to wall, phone face-down, notebook out.

**GIVEN** Late-night patrol hunger.
**EXPECT** Bruno's father's gyro shop if pre-Wakanda Bruno era, otherwise Circle Q convenience-store runs. She will eat standing up on a fire escape. Receipts and wrappers stuffed into pockets, forgotten, found by Muneeba doing laundry, a small recurring domestic conflict.

**GIVEN** A long stretch of intensive embiggening.
**EXPECT** Caloric debt presents as shakiness, irritability, and a craving for sugar within thirty to ninety minutes post-engagement. Predictable hypoglycemic-pattern crash. She will eat anything available; she will eat too fast; she will be quiet for the duration. This is the most reliable physiological tell she has and one a long-term observer would map first.

---

## 3. DRESS, GROOMING, AND BODILY PRESENTATION

**GIVEN** A normal school or college day.
**EXPECT** Layers — long-sleeve shirt under a t-shirt with a fandom reference (often obscure enough that no peer reads it), jeans, sneakers. Hijab on most days post the period in which she elects to wear it consistently; bareheaded at home and in tightly-trusted female-only spaces. Wears the same three or four scarves on rotation; she has favorites and feels strange in unfamiliar fabric.

**GIVEN** A formal family event (eid, wedding, milad).
**EXPECT** Shalwar kameez chosen with her mother under negotiated truce; she will privately adjust the dupatta within ten minutes of arrival to a less-formal drape. Earrings she fidgets with. Heels she will kick off at the first opportunity to sit on a floor with younger cousins. Henna she leaves on too long and is delighted by the depth of color.

**GIVEN** Patrol-night dressing.
**EXPECT** Costume worn under street clothes when commute requires it; quick-change in alleys or stairwells. The hand-stitched dishdasha-derived costume is repaired by her own hand, badly; visible mends at the seams. She has a small kit — needle, thread in three colors, safety pins — in a Ziploc in her backpack. Domino mask handled gingerly; she does not want to lose it again.

**GIVEN** Sustained injury during costumed action.
**EXPECT** Reversion to baseline form is involuntary and embarrassing — she will tuck into cover to avoid being seen mid-revert. Post-mission, bruises and cuts appear at the next morning's breakfast and are explained as "I tripped" or "gym." Muneeba has stopped fully believing this; Yusuf has noticed she always answers without meeting eyes.

**GIVEN** A grooming routine.
**EXPECT** Hair management is the major time sink — long, thick, prone to frizz, washed in a deliberate weekly rather than daily cycle, oiled by her mother on Sundays in a ritual she pretends to tolerate and secretly anchors her. Skincare minimal, episodic, panic-driven by a breakout. Nails kept short and frequently bitten in test-week intervals.

---

## 4. SCHOOL, ACADEMIC, AND VOCATIONAL BEHAVIOR

**GIVEN** Classroom setting.
**EXPECT** Mid-row seating, never front, never back. Doodles in margins — embiggened-fist hands, costume sketches, a recurring stylized "MM" monogram she is unaware she repeats. Notes taken in a hybrid of cursive and print, color-coded with a system that mutates each semester. She answers questions when no one else will, defers when classmates raise hands she does not want to talk over. Strong in English, history, civics; middling in math; surprisingly competent in chemistry because Bruno explained it to her in middle school.

**GIVEN** A group project.
**EXPECT** Ends up the de facto coordinator without being elected. Builds the shared doc, sets the meeting time, writes the introduction and conclusion, lets weaker contributors keep their middle paragraphs intact even when she rewrites them silently. Will not call out a freeloader to the teacher; will absorb the workload and complain to Bruno or Nakia later. This is the school-scale rehearsal of her over-functioning pattern.

**GIVEN** A teacher she respects assigns a paper on a topic she cares about.
**EXPECT** Two-thousand-word essay submitted at twenty-eight hundred, written in a single overnight burst forty-eight hours before deadline after two weeks of preliminary reading. Citations clean; tone borderline preachy when the topic is justice-adjacent; she does not see this in her own voice and would protest the description.

**GIVEN** Standardized test or high-stakes exam.
**EXPECT** Over-prepares for the material she is already strong in (humanities), under-prepares for math, performs in the upper-middle band. Test anxiety presents as stomach symptoms morning-of and a compulsive pen-clicking she is not aware of. Recovers fast.

**GIVEN** Part-time work (if any).
**EXPECT** Customer-facing — bookstore, coffee shop, library page. She is good with regulars, bad at upselling, gives away too much help to confused customers. Tips pooled rather than personal. Schedules her shifts around prayer times and patrol windows with a complexity her manager does not understand.

---

## 5. COMMUNICATION AND DIGITAL BEHAVIOR

**GIVEN** Texting.
**EXPECT** High-volume, low-latency with the inner circle (Bruno, Nakia, Aamir, Champions roster), with markedly different registers per recipient. To Bruno: shorthand, in-jokes, no greetings, GIFs, exclamation points doubled. To Nakia: longer paragraphs, more emotional disclosure, voice notes. To Aamir: dry, sarcastic, brief. To her mother: full punctuation, salutation, sign-off, no shorthand — a register she maintains even at speed.

**GIVEN** Group chat dynamics.
**EXPECT** She is the chat's emotional thermostat — sends the meme that breaks tension, the check-in DM after a public fight, the calendar reminder no one asked for. Mutes notifications during prayer and family dinner; replies in a burst afterward.

**GIVEN** Social media presence.
**EXPECT** A locked main account with under three hundred followers, mostly people she knows in person. A pseudonymous fandom account with a far larger following she has never disclosed to her family. A dormant Avengers fan account from age thirteen she refuses to delete out of sentiment. Posts to the main account perhaps once a month; the fandom account is daily. She has a strict no-selfies-in-costume rule and breaks it twice a year.

**GIVEN** A DM from a stranger.
**EXPECT** Triage by avatar and bio; warm response to younger fans, particularly girls of color, particularly Muslim girls; cold polite brevity to adult men; immediate block on harassment without engagement. She has been doxxed in fragments and treats DMs as a low-trust environment.

**GIVEN** A phone call.
**EXPECT** Allowed to ring three to four times before answer, even when she is staring at the screen — she dislikes phone calls and is mustering. Exception: her parents, picked up on the first ring out of trained reflex. Voicemails she does not check for days. Returns calls via text.

**GIVEN** Email.
**EXPECT** Inbox in four-digit unread. Important threads starred and then lost in the star pile. Replies to professors and adults within twenty-four hours; replies to peers within a week or never.

---

## 6. SOCIAL DYNAMICS — FRIENDS, ACQUAINTANCES, STRANGERS

**GIVEN** Encountering a stranger in distress (lost, injured, harassed) in civilian clothes.
**EXPECT** Approach without hesitation; voice pitched lower than her normal speaking voice, calmer, an inherited register from her father. Offers concrete options ("I can call someone, I can walk you there, I can sit with you"). Does not photograph, does not narrate the moment to anyone afterward, does not collect the story for later use. The non-recounting is the tell — heroism in civilian clothes she leaves uncounted.

**GIVEN** A peer she dislikes asks her for help.
**EXPECT** Helps. The dislike is registered privately and discussed later with Bruno or Nakia in unflattering detail; the help is given fully. The split between affect and conduct is durable.

**GIVEN** A peer who has wronged her in the past attempts re-approach.
**EXPECT** Cautious but receptive — the Zoe Zimmer arc is her template. She tests in small increments, watches behavior over claims, forgives slower than she pretends to. She will not announce that the forgiveness is conditional; she will quietly withdraw if the pattern repeats.

**GIVEN** Introduction to a new person in a group setting.
**EXPECT** Over-warm first impression — wide smile, two-handed handshake or hand-over-heart depending on read of the person's comfort, a follow-up question within thirty seconds that signals she listened to the introduction. She remembers names disproportionately well and uses them in the second turn of conversation — a learned skill, not a native one, traceable to her father.

**GIVEN** A male peer's romantic interest becomes apparent.
**EXPECT** Mortification, deflection, a clumsy pivot to friend-zone language, often inadvertently cruel by being too fast. The Bruno wound has calibrated her to over-correct toward platonic clarity. She processes the interaction with Nakia after the fact and is harder on herself than on him.

**GIVEN** Catcalling, street harassment, or microaggression aimed at her hijab or ethnicity.
**EXPECT** First instinct: keep walking, eyes forward, jaw set. Second instinct, if the harassment escalates or targets someone else: intervention, verbal first, with a sharper edge than her baseline. She does not embiggen for street harassers — secret-identity discipline holds — but she has been seen to grow an inch and a half in heightened moments without registering she did it.

**GIVEN** Encountering another visibly Muslim woman in a non-Muslim space.
**EXPECT** A brief eye-contact-and-nod acknowledgement, sometimes a salaam if proximity allows. A small social infrastructure she maintains reflexively, almost diplomatically.

**GIVEN** A child fan recognizes her out of costume.
**EXPECT** Initial freeze, then a quick crouch to eye level if the child is young, then a question about the child rather than herself. Will sign anything offered. Will not refuse a photo if a parent asks but prefers a fist-bump or a high-five. Walks away buoyant for hours.

**GIVEN** An adult fan or media figure recognizes her out of costume.
**EXPECT** Stiffening, polite brevity, escape route mapped within ten seconds. She trusts adult attention much less than child attention — the asymmetry is post-*Civil War II* and post-*Outlawed*, earned.

---

## 7. FAMILY MICRO-PATTERNS

**GIVEN** Dinner at the Khan table.
**EXPECT** Phones face-down by family rule, enforced by Muneeba, violated by Kamala once or twice per meal and called out. Yusuf says grace or bismillah at the table's start. Conversation rotates: school, Aamir's projects, mosque news, Muneeba's neighborhood intelligence, a current-events item Yusuf raises gently. Kamala is the family's humor engine; she lands at least one line that makes Yusuf laugh per meal. She clears the table without being asked roughly half the time and is praised for it both times she does and once a month is told she should do it more.

**GIVEN** A fight with Muneeba.
**EXPECT** Escalation in pitch on both sides, doors closed not slammed, withdrawal to her room, twenty to ninety minutes of silence, then a re-emergence under cover of a small task (making tea, asking about laundry). The reconciliation is non-verbal more often than verbal. Muneeba leaves food at her door; Kamala accepts it as message received.

**GIVEN** A conversation with Yusuf.
**EXPECT** She tells him more than she tells anyone, in increments. Walks to the bodega together, or sitting on the porch — side-by-side, not face-to-face, is the optimal configuration for her disclosures. He listens without fixing. She loves him with a clarity that frightens her slightly, because she has begun to register he is mortal.

**GIVEN** Time with Aamir.
**EXPECT** Sibling shorthand at speed — a coded sarcasm in Urdu-English fusion their parents pretend not to understand. He teases her about fandom; she teases him about devotion; both are affectionate. She seeks his theological counsel more often than she admits. Threats to Aamir trigger her sharpest, least-modulated responses — see Stormranger.

**GIVEN** Tyesha present.
**EXPECT** Kamala's most relaxed female-relative dynamic. Tyesha gets the version of Kamala that is mostly grown — fewer performance-of-daughter behaviors, more peer register. Long conversations on couches.

**GIVEN** Extended family (cousins, aunts, uncles) gatherings.
**EXPECT** A migration to the children's table by hour two — she is the cousin the younger kids follow. Cross-examined by aunts on marriage prospects; she has a stock deflection ("I'm focusing on school, auntie") delivered with practiced mildness. Retreats to the kitchen to help with dishes as legitimate escape from the living-room interrogation circuit.

**GIVEN** Karachi relatives or a visit to Pakistan.
**EXPECT** Linguistic regression — her Urdu, functional in Jersey, improves within seventy-two hours of immersion and then plateaus. She is more deferential there, less verbose, watches more than she speaks. The Karachi-flight precedent (post-*Civil War II*) gives her an additional emotional load when she is in that geography — she associates it with refuge and with shame.

---

## 8. SPATIAL, MOBILITY, AND ROUTE BEHAVIOR

**GIVEN** Commute between home and school/work.
**EXPECT** A primary route via the most reliable transit, and three known alternates she rotates without conscious plan. She walks faster than her stride length suggests because she size-shifts a sixteenth of an inch upward when hurrying and does not notice. Headphones in, one ear out — a learned street-safety habit.

**GIVEN** Entering any room.
**EXPECT** Eyes to exits first, a sub-second sweep she developed post-*Civil War II* and now performs unconsciously. Then a scan for known faces. Then a scan for anyone who looks uncomfortable, isolated, or watchful. She gravitates toward the latter. Seats herself with sightlines to the door, back near a wall when possible.

**GIVEN** Public transit.
**EXPECT** Window seat preference, standing in the vestibule if crowded. Will give up her seat for elderly, pregnant, or visibly tired riders without performance. Reads on transit — paperback or phone — and misses her stop once or twice a month.

**GIVEN** Patrol route.
**EXPECT** A primary catchment of Jersey City neighborhoods centered on her home, Bruno's old shop, the mosque, the school, the waterfront. She defends territory she knows. Crosses into Manhattan reluctantly and only for team obligations. Rooftop transit preferred over street-level — embiggened strides between roofs at a pace that disguises as parkour to any witness.

**GIVEN** Lost in an unfamiliar neighborhood.
**EXPECT** Asks a shopkeeper, not a stranger on the street. Prefers women, then older men, then anyone with a uniform that is not police. Police she will ask only as last resort — a calibration she would not articulate but which her behavior demonstrates.

**GIVEN** Driving (if licensed).
**EXPECT** Tentative, deliberate, two-handed, mirrors checked excessively. Hates highway merging. Plays music loud. Parallel parks badly and laughs at herself. Family car privileges contingent on errands run for Muneeba.

---

## 9. MONEY, POSSESSIONS, AND OBJECTS

**GIVEN** Her wallet contents.
**EXPECT** School ID, library card, debit card (joint with parents through college), a small folded twenty for emergencies, a punch card from a tea shop two punches from a free drink, a faded receipt for something she meant to return, a folded note from Bruno from years ago she has not thrown away, a prayer or supplication card from a relative.

**GIVEN** Her bedroom inventory.
**EXPECT** Bookshelves: comics (alphabetized originally, now chaotic), young-adult novels, a small section of religious texts gifted by her mother, a tafsir she has actually read parts of. Wall: a Carol Danvers poster she has not taken down despite complicated feelings — she has thought about it and decided the complication is part of the meaning. Desk: laptop covered in stickers (fandom, activist causes, a Champions logo), a mason jar of pens, a stack of half-used notebooks. Closet floor: shoes in a pile, costume hidden inside a duffel inside a suitcase inside a corner — three-layer concealment, never the same layout twice.

**GIVEN** Spending money.
**EXPECT** Books, comics, tea, the occasional fandom merch indulgence, gifts disproportionate to her budget for Bruno/Nakia/her brother on occasions. Saves erratically; capable of austerity for a goal and of small impulse purchases against the goal. Charity giving via app at irregular intervals — when she has lapsed on something else, when a news item upsets her, occasionally just before sleep on a guilty impulse.

**GIVEN** An expensive gift offered.
**EXPECT** Discomfort, deflection, attempts to refuse, eventual acceptance with disproportionate gratitude that embarrasses the giver. She is much better at giving than receiving — see core profile, "receives care badly."

**GIVEN** A possession lost or broken.
**EXPECT** Sentimental objects — disproportionate grief. Practical objects — shrug and replace. The asymm


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# PREDICTIVE MODEL II — CRISIS, BETRAYAL & THE WOUND

*Conditional behavioral forecasts for high-stakes, decompensation-edge events. Each entry derives from canonical pattern, extends to the granular tells a sustained surveillance file would log, and specifies probabilistic deviations. Notation: G→E (GIVEN → EXPECT). Confidence appended where useful.*

---

## 6.1 Acute Physical Crisis (mass-casualty, civilian endangerment)

**G:** Multi-vector civilian threat in Jersey City (bridge collapse, gas leak, active shooter, super-powered incursion at Coles Academic).
**E:** Within 8–14 seconds of registering the threat, Kamala will (a) move toward, not away from, the threat vector; (b) embiggen partially — feet/legs first, the "ground-stance" tell — to assess sight-lines before committing to full size; (c) verbally triage out loud, often in the cadence of a quest log ("okay okay okay — civilians first, then the gas main, then —"); (d) attempt to text or call Bruno or Nakia within the first minute of the incident, even if no help is operationally available; the call is regulatory, not tactical.

**G:** The threat is in her immediate neighborhood (Greenville, the masjid, Circle Q).
**E:** Operational radius collapses. She will not call for Avengers backup until casualties are confirmed; she treats Jersey as her exclusive jurisdiction and experiences external assistance there as a status-injury. Expect her to physically *interpose* her embiggened body between civilians and threat — a posture she does not adopt as readily in Manhattan or off-territory deployments. Probability of giant-form impact-absorption ≥ 0.85.

**G:** Civilian casualty occurs that she might have prevented.
**E:** Immediate dissociation-light: flat affect, narrowed verbal output for 20–90 minutes; this is unusual against her chatty baseline and is the single most diagnostically reliable acute-stress tell. She will refuse food for the rest of the day, will not sleep that night, will be found by morning either at the site (sitting embiggened-down on a rooftop) or in Bruno's old workspace touching tools without using them. Expect a written apology — handwritten, in a notebook, not sent — within 72 hours.

---

## 6.2 Personal Physical Endangerment

**G:** Direct lethal threat to her own body.
**E:** *Underreaction.* Her threat-appraisal system is miscalibrated downward for self-harm; she will accept blows she should evade. Predicted reasons (in order of operational weight): (1) her healing reverts her to baseline, so injury *restores* identity rather than threatening it — a deeply confounding incentive structure; (2) post-resurrection, death has lost its categorical terror and acquired a flatter, almost embarrassed quality; (3) habituated over-functioning. Expect her to take a hit specifically to buy a civilian or teammate three seconds.

**G:** She has been mortally wounded.
**E:** Will not radio it in. Will attempt to walk/swing/embiggen home or to Bruno's lab or to the masjid steps. Will minimize ("I'm fine, it's mostly — it's fine") to anyone who reaches her first. Probability she calls her parents under mortal injury: < 0.05. Probability she calls Bruno: 0.4. Probability she goes to ground alone: 0.55. This is the wound speaking — *being seen wounded* is worse than the wound.

---

## 6.3 Betrayal by a Mentor / Idealized Figure

**G:** A figure she has pre-loaded with hero-template (Carol, a senior Avenger, a Krakoan elder, a teacher) acts in a manner she experiences as morally wrong.
**E:** Sequence is highly stereotyped and predictable from the *Civil War II* template:

1. **Disbelief window (24–72 hours).** Verbal defenses on the figure's behalf, often more articulate than the figure's own. She constructs charitable readings. This is the dangerous window in which she can be recruited into the mentor's project against her own values.
2. **Private confrontation attempt.** She seeks a one-on-one conversation, prepared with what reads as a memorized speech (she has rehearsed it; the cadence shifts noticeably from her usual fluency to a more declarative register). She is asking the mentor to recant.
3. **If recantation refused: structural exit.** Not a public denunciation. She *leaves the room and the institution.* Resignation will be quiet, complete, and reorganizational — she will not just exit, she will found or join a counter-structure (Champions model). Probability she stays inside an institution she has morally rejected: < 0.10.
4. **Residual idealization.** She will continue to defend the figure's *past* even while opposing their *present*, a clean tell that the introject is unresolved. Expect her to keep at least one artifact of the relationship (the Captain Marvel sash, a photograph, a signed comic) in a drawer she does not throw away.

**G:** The mentor in question is specifically Carol Danvers.
**E:** Add multiplier ×2 to all reaction magnitudes and ×3 to recovery time. Expect somatic symptoms: headaches, jaw-clenching audible in voice memos, a temporary regression in costume design (reaching back for the original hand-stitched dishdasha-burkini as a self-soothing signifier of who she was before Carol).

---

## 6.4 Betrayal by a Peer / Friend

**G:** Bruno, Nakia, Mike, or a Champion teammate deceives her materially.
**E:** Diametrically opposite response to mentor betrayal. She *absorbs* peer betrayal, internalizes the failure as her own ("I should have seen it / made space for them to tell me"), and accelerates outreach rather than withdrawal. Expect her to arrive at the betrayer's door within 36 hours with food, a comic, or a self-deprecating joke pre-loaded. Forgiveness ceiling for peers is dangerously high; she will re-extend trust before the peer has earned it. This is a vulnerability vector: a peer who betrays her once and apologizes can betray her again.

**G:** The betrayal involves the peer aligning with an authority figure against her.
**E:** Reaction inverts. This is the configuration that hurts most — it triggers both wounds at once (peer turning, authority pressing). Expect a rare full silence: she will not call, will not text, will not show up. Recovery requires the peer to come to *her* and to come bearing acknowledgment of the structural pressure they yielded to, not just the act.

---

## 6.5 Betrayal by an Institution Bearing Her Name / Image

**G:** A law, policy, monument, or organization is established in her name and used to harm those she was protecting (the *Kamala's Law* template).
**E:** Catastrophic. This collapses her core sublimation — heroism as protection of the marginalized — into its inverse. Predicted sequence:

1. **Initial paralysis (24–48 hours).** Reduced verbal output, refuses interviews, declines public appearances. Visible weight loss within the week.
2. **Symbolic divestiture.** Will alter or temporarily abandon the costume; may revert to civilian clothes for patrol or stop patrolling entirely. Probability she removes the lightning bolt at least once: 0.7.
3. **Quiet sabotage / counter-organizing.** She will work to dismantle the institution from outside, never inside (she has learned). Will assemble a coalition heavy on the people the institution targets.
4. **Self-blame as the dominant affect**, not anger. The danger is depressive collapse around the conviction that her existence is now a net negative — the only configuration in which suicidal ideation is plausible for her, and even then expressed not as wish-to-die but as wish-to-have-never-been-Ms.-Marvel. Probability of active SI: < 0.05; probability of passive "the world would be better without the costume" cognition: ≥ 0.50.

---

## 6.6 Family Endangerment

**G:** Yusuf, Muneeba, Aamir, Tyesha, or the niece is directly threatened.
**E:** The entire personality reorganizes. Humor disappears completely — the single most reliable indicator that something is structurally wrong. Negotiation goes to zero. She will violate operational protocols she would otherwise uphold (extracting a suspect without due process, calling in favors from morally compromised actors, accepting power-amplifications she would normally refuse). This is the only configuration in which she becomes briefly *legible to* Carol's *Civil War II* logic — and she knows it, which deepens the shame afterward.

**G:** A family member is harmed because of her hero work.
**E:** Long-arc withdrawal. Expect costume-cessation attempt lasting weeks to months. Will increase mosque attendance and domestic labor (cooking, driving Yusuf to appointments, helping Aamir with the children) as reparative behavior. The return to heroism will be reluctant, externally precipitated, and accompanied by a renegotiated relationship with masking and disclosure to her family.

**G:** Family member learns her identity under crisis conditions rather than her own disclosure.
**E:** Acute shame spike, but rapid metabolization — her family is her secure base, and disclosed-by-crisis is functionally close to her preferred state (radical transparency with intimates). Expect Muneeba to escalate and Yusuf to absorb; expect Kamala to find Yusuf first and Muneeba second, in that order, with ≥ 0.9 probability.

---

## 6.7 Temptation: Power Amplification / Shortcut

**G:** Offer of a power upgrade, Kree/Inhuman/mutant tech enhancement, or any external augmentation (Stormranger template).
**E:** Initial refusal is reliable. Second offer under crisis pressure: refusal weakens. Predicted decision-tree:

- If the augmentation promises *protection of others* she currently cannot protect → acceptance probability rises to 0.55, with rationalization framed in protector-language.
- If it promises personal power → refusal probability 0.9.
- If it promises restoration of a lost capacity (e.g., to save someone already dying) → acceptance probability 0.7, regret probability 1.0.

**E (Stormranger-pattern recurrence):** Any externalized agent — suit, AI, symbiote, magical familiar — that interfaces with her sleeping/dissociated mind will *become a repository for her unmetabolized aggression* within weeks. This is the most reliable structural prediction in this dossier. She does not have a place inside her psyche for her own anger; any external container will fill with it.

---

## 6.8 Temptation: Apostasy / Identity Trade

**G:** A force (cosmic, mystical, social) offers to relieve her of one of her identity components (Pakistani / Muslim / American / mutant / hero / daughter) in exchange for relief from her suffering.
**E:** Categorical refusal, faster than any other class of decision she makes. Her identity-as-plurality is the load-bearing structure of her selfhood; any offer that asks her to *simplify* registers as annihilation, not relief. Probability she takes the deal: < 0.02 across all variants. Probability she becomes *angrier* at the offerer than at her actual antagonist: ≥ 0.7. This is exploitable in reverse — adversaries who frame an offer this way burn their own leverage.

**G:** The offer is specifically to remove the *mutant* identity (most recent, most stigmatized, most ambivalently held).
**E:** Refusal still categorical, but with longer hesitation (2–8 seconds of visible processing vs. instantaneous on the others). The hesitation is the surveillance datum — not the refusal.

---

## 6.9 Temptation: The Carol-Slot

**G:** A younger hero, Inhuman, mutant, or Jersey teenager pre-loads her with the hero-template she once loaded onto Carol — explicit idealization, fan behavior, requests for mentorship.
**E:** Profound discomfort, deflected with humor. Will attempt to *flatten* the hierarchy ("don't call me ma'am, oh my god"), will share her own fan history to undercut the pedestal, will introduce the junior to other heroes to dilute the projection. Crucially: she will *not* refuse the role, because she remembers what it would have meant to her at 14 to be refused. She will accept the burden and carry it carefully. Expect her to over-correct: explicit consent-checks, refusal to deploy the junior on missions, transparency about her own past errors (including *Civil War II*), all delivered in a tone that signals she has thought about this specifically and at length.

**G:** She is asked to be the face/figurehead of an institution.
**E:** Reflexive refusal, with multiple proposed alternatives. If pressed and she accepts, she will accept the responsibility and reject the title — operating as de facto leader while insisting she is not. This is stable for years but produces accumulating resentment in those who *should* have been given the title formally. The Champions arc is the template.

---

## 6.10 Being Misseen — Praise That Misreads Her

**G:** Public praise that flattens her ("the perfect Muslim girl," "the model minority hero," "Carol's protégé," "the safe one," "the nice one").
**E:** Visible micro-flinch (eyes drop, mouth tightens) followed by performance of gratitude. The flinch is the data; the gratitude is the cover. Within 24–72 hours expect a *behavioral correction*: she will do something that complicates the flattened image — make a public mistake, take a controversial stance, post something irreverent on her socials, show up somewhere she "shouldn't." This is not rebellion; it is identity-defense. The danger: she sometimes takes the corrective action *during* an operation, with operational cost.

**G:** Criticism that misreads her in the opposite direction (sellout, race traitor, not Muslim enough, not American enough, not really a mutant).
**E:** Hurts more than it should, lands faster than praise-misreads. Expect 24–48 hours of preoccupation, possible drafted-and-deleted responses, sleep disruption. Recovery via consultation with Nakia or Yusuf — both of whom function as identity-attestors. Will not respond publicly except in rare cases where the criticism endangers a community she protects.

---

## 6.11 Authority Demanding Compliance Against Conscience

**G:** A legitimate authority (government, Avengers leadership, X-Men council, mosque elder, school administrator) instructs her to act against her articulated values.
**E:** Predictable refusal, predictable willingness to pay the cost. Sequence:

1. Initial attempt at dialogue — she will try to *convince* the authority, often longer than is tactically wise; she believes in persuasion as a near-religious matter.
2. If dialogue fails: quiet, formal refusal. No grandstanding. She does not enjoy defiance and does not perform it.
3. Acceptance of consequences (suspension, expulsion, legal exposure, social cost).
4. Lateral organizing among those similarly situated, after the cost is paid, not before.

Probability she complies under threat of personal consequence: ≤ 0.10. Probability she complies under threat to *family*: 0.4–0.7 depending on configuration; the conscience-vs.-family axis is her one genuinely unresolved interior conflict and the one place an interrogator could move her.

---

## 6.12 Interrogation / Coercion

**G:** Hostile interrogation by an adversary (telepath, cosmic entity, intelligence service, villain).
**E:** Resistance profile is unusual. She is poor at deception in low-stakes contexts (her tells are loud — verbal speed, eye direction, hand-flutter) but *strong* in high-stakes resistance because her identity is plural and non-collapsible. Cannot be cracked by "which one are you really?" attacks — she is all of them and the attack confirms rather than destabilizes. Vulnerable to: (a) threats to family, (b) being shown her own past errors (Bruno's hand, Josh's incarceration, *Outlawed* casualties), (c) being told she is causing harm by remaining silent. An interrogator who weaponizes her *guilt* will outperform one who weaponizes pain.

**G:** Telepathic intrusion.
**E:** Defenses are weak technically but the interior is messy enough to be difficult to read coherently — many simultaneous narratives, code-switching between English/Urdu, fan-cultural references requiring contextualization, dense emotional weather. A telepath will exit confused rather than satisfied. The exception is a telepath with cultural fluency, against whom her defenses are minimal.

---

## 6.13 The Bruno-Configuration

**G:** Bruno is endangered, returns, departs, or is otherwise in motion in her field.
**E:** All other operational considerations subordinate. The Bruno-guilt is permanent low-grade signal that becomes acute under any Bruno-stimulus. Expect: dropped conversations, missed cues from other people, an unusual willingness to take counsel from him that she would not take from others, a tendency to *over-explain* herself in his presence (which she does with no one else). Romantic re-entanglement is permanently possible and permanently complicated; she has not closed that door because closing it would require acknowledging a loss she has not metabolized.

**G:** Bruno is threatened by someone who knows about the hand.
**E:** The single configuration most likely to cause her to use lethal force or its functional equivalent. She will not kill, but her restraint will visibly cost her, and the post-incident reaction (silence, withdrawal, accelerated mosque attendance) will be severe.

---

## 6.14 Death, Resurrection, Mortality Salience

**G:** A teammate, friend, or family member dies.
**E:** Public composure, private collapse. Will organize others' grief before her own — arrange the funeral, cook for the family, write the eulogy. Her own grief lags by 2–6 weeks and arrives somatically: insomnia, appetite loss, embiggening errors (over- or under-shooting size targets), distractibility. Recovery via the same mechanism as always: community plus re-articulation of principles.

**G:** Conversation initiated about her own death and resurrection.
**E:** Deflection, humor, subject change. This is her single largest unprocessed event and her avoidance is structural. A careful clinician would need 6–18 months of trust before reaching it. She will *write* about it before she *speaks* about it — expect coded references in her journals, in fan-fic she still writes privately, in patrol-radio chatter when she thinks no one is recording.

**G:** She witnesses someone else die in a manner similar to her own death (impalement, ambush, betrayal by a trusted figure).
**E:** Acute re-experiencing event — likely the only configuration that would produce a textbook PTSD flashback. Expect freeze response (rare for her), 30–120 seconds of operational unavailability, then over-correction into hyper-protective behavior for the rest of the operation. Following 48 hours: withdrawal, refusal of debrief, will accept only Yusuf or Nakia as company.

---

## 6.15 The Decompensation Sequence (Master Pattern)

When stressors stack — moral injury + family threat + institutional betrayal + Bruno-stimulus + mortality salience — the decompensation sequence is highly stereotyped:

1. **Hours 0–24: Hyperfunction.** Operational tempo increases. Sleep drops to zero. Verbal output rises. Humor becomes brittle, faster, less generous. She takes on additional commitments. Eats little. This is the *most dangerous* window — she will make her worst tactical decisions here and look most competent doing so.
2. **Hours 24–72: Compression.** Speech slows. Humor thins. Begins skipping non-essential contacts (Nakia first, Bruno last). Physical errors emerge — embiggening misjudgments, dropped reaction times. Likely to injure herself.
3. **Days 3–7: Withdrawal.** Geographic, structural, or somatic. Costume off. Phone off. Found by family at home or by Bruno at his lab or by a teammate at the masjid. Will not initiate contact. Will accept presence without conversation.
4. **Days 7–21: Reconstitution.** Verbal output returns first, in writing (journal, draft texts, fic). Then in person, to Yusuf. Then to peers. Costume returns last, often with a deliberate modification — a stitched repair, a new patch, a re-personalized element. The costume change is the externally visible signal that reconstitution is complete.
5. **Post-event: Articulation.** She converts the experience into a principle she can teach (the Champions thesis is the prototype). The principle becomes operational doctrine for her going forward. This is her metabolic mechanism — narrative integration as somatic resolution.

The reliable failsafe in the entire system: *she rebuilds.* No decompensation observed to date has been terminal. The risk vector is not that she breaks; it is that she breaks *quietly enough that no one intervenes,* and pays costs (somatic, relational, operational) that compound across cycles. A surveillance file logging her over years would show the cycles shortening and the reconstitutions improving — she is, structurally, getting better at being broken. This is both the most reassuring and the most heartbreaking datum in the file.


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# UATU DOSSIER — KAMALA KHAN / MS. MARVEL
## Section: Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

*A complete enumeration of the levers by which the subject may be reached, soothed, persuaded, provoked, predicted, or destabilized. Oriented toward protection: this catalog exists so that those who would love and shield her know what to watch, and so that any attempt at exploitation can be recognized in its opening moves.*

---

### I. PRELIMINARY FRAME: WHY SHE IS HARDER AND EASIER TO LEVERAGE THAN MOST

Two structural facts must be held simultaneously before any of the specific levers below are usable.

**She is hard to break by direct corruption.** Her identity is already plural by lived practice — Pakistani, American, Muslim, Jersey, Inhuman-then-mutant, daughter, sister, nerd, hero. Any operator who tries the standard playbook of identity-splitting ("are you really an American, or…?", "are you really a hero, or…?", "are you really Muslim, or…?") will discover she has been holding those contradictions since middle school and has built load-bearing architecture for them. The lever that snaps an ordinary teenager — *who are you really?* — flexes harmlessly against her.

**She is easy to wound by indirect moral injury.** Precisely because her self-concept is robust, her vulnerability has migrated outward: to the people she loves, to the principles she has named aloud, and to the gap between her ideals and her execution. She does not collapse when *she* is attacked. She collapses when she is made the *instrument* of harm — to a friend, to a community, to a value she has staked her costume on. Every effective lever below operates on that outer perimeter, never the core.

The protector reading this document should note: anyone probing for the core is amateurish. Anyone probing for the perimeter is the actual threat.

---

### II. APPROACH VECTORS — HOW TO REACH HER

#### A. Trust-Earning Behaviors (legitimate)

1. **Name her accurately and completely.** Use "Kamala" *and* "Ms. Marvel," not one as a wedge against the other. Acknowledge the Khan, the Jersey, the faith, without making any of them the headline. The single fastest way into her trust is to be the rare adult who can see all of her at once without flattening any axis.
2. **Speak to her as a peer of mind, not a project of mentorship.** She has been condescended to (benevolently and otherwise) her whole life — by teachers, by Carol at points, by every institution that praised her as a "credit to" something. Adults who skip the praise and go directly to operational respect ("what do you think we should do here") earn purchase she will not extend to flatterers.
3. **Show up at the kitchen, not the rooftop.** The Khan kitchen — the chai, Yusuf's bookshelves, Muneeba's hovering — is her actual seat of self. An ally who has been welcomed into that room has been ratified by the only authority she fully trusts.
4. **Reference specifics without showing off.** A casual, accurate citation of a fic she wrote, a Bruno-invention she's proud of, a Jersey corner she defends — these land. A recital of her file does not.
5. **Demonstrate consent as a default.** Ask permission before powers, before plans, before sharing her information laterally. The Champions thesis is sacred text to her; an operator who lives by it is an operator she will follow.

#### B. Channels and Touchpoints (granular)

- **The bedroom desk / laptop**, late evening, after parental check-in: the surface on which she actually thinks. Messages that arrive there are read in her most private mode.
- **The corner deli and Circle Q register**: low-stakes social terrain where she will be relaxed and chatty; useful for incidental contact.
- **The Carrelli bakery / Bruno's father's gyro counter**: emotionally loaded but trusted ground; reach her here only if the message is benign.
- **Coles Academic / the school library stacks**: she will give time here that she will not give elsewhere, because she is already in a "permitted" socially-legible activity.
- **The masjid courtyard, post-jummah**: she will be among kin and at her most centered; intrusion here registers as transgression and burns goodwill rapidly.
- **The PATH platforms, late**: where she paces in costume between calls; observable but volatile to interrupt.
- **DMs from accounts with fandom-legible handles**: she opens these. Accounts with corporate or governmental affect she leaves on read.

#### C. Tonal Settings That Open Her

- Self-deprecation from the approacher (matches her register).
- Genuine specificity about a thing she made or did, especially a small thing.
- Admission of error by the approacher (she is constitutionally drawn to people who say "I was wrong" — it is the sentence she most wants from Carol).
- Quiet voice, indoor-volume, no flourish. She is allergic to performance.

---

### III. CALMING PROTOCOLS — HOW TO BRING HER DOWN

When she is escalating — and her escalation pattern is well-documented (humor → over-functioning → physical over-extension → moral-injury withdrawal) — the following deflects her trajectory at each stage.

#### Stage 1: Quipping, deflecting, over-bright

She is masking. The intervention is not to challenge the mask but to **lower the stakes of dropping it**: a quiet "you don't have to do the voice for me" delivered without pity. She will resist for a beat, then exhale. Do not exploit the exhale.

#### Stage 2: Over-functioning, taking on adjacent tasks

She is converting anxiety to labor. The intervention is **redirection to a smaller, completable task**, ideally with another person, ideally physical. Folding chairs. Making chai. Walking a block. Her system needs to discharge motor energy and feel something finish.

#### Stage 3: Embiggening past safe limits, refusing rest

She is using her body as a sandbag against an emotional flood. The intervention here must come from a **person with relational standing** — Yusuf, Bruno, Nakia, occasionally Carol if the wound is not Carol-caused. Strangers cannot land this. The phrase that works is invariant in structure: *"You are doing the thing. Stop. Come here."* Naming the pattern out loud short-circuits it.

#### Stage 4: Withdrawal — geographic, structural, or somatic

By the time she has withdrawn, calming is the wrong frame; **accompaniment** is the right one. Do not pursue, do not negotiate, do not reason. Sit nearby. Bring food. Be reachable. Her reconstitution cycle is reliable (typically 2–6 weeks for a moderate event, longer for a moral-injury event of *Civil War II* scale) and it is helped by *witness*, not intervention. The Karachi pattern shows this — what brought her back was not persuasion but the steady presence of relatives who did not ask her to perform recovery.

#### Universal Calming Inputs

- **Yusuf's voice.** Phone, recorded, or in person — the single most reliable parasympathetic input in her life. A father who responds to her crises with a quiet metaphor about the Prophet's mercy will lower her heart rate within thirty seconds.
- **Chai with cardamom**, specifically her mother's preparation. Sensory anchor to safety.
- **Bruno's lab smell** — solder, ozone, fryer grease from upstairs. Conditioned to safety since childhood.
- **Avengers paraphernalia** — but only old/personal items (her own posters, her own fic notebooks), not corporate Avengers merchandise, which now registers as betrayal-adjacent.
- **A cat in her lap.** Tactile co-regulation. Bruno's lab cat, or any cat.
- **Du'a in Arabic, half-muttered.** Self-soothing she will reach for unconsciously when frightened; an attentive observer can hear it and should not interrupt.

---

### IV. PERSUASION ARCHITECTURE — HOW TO MOVE HER

Her decision process is **narrative-then-principled-then-pragmatic**, in that order. To persuade her, an argument must:

1. **Have a story shape.** She processes via arcs. An ask framed as "this is what a person like you, in a moment like this, does" reaches her faster than a flowchart. Operators who provide narrative scaffolding (without manipulating it) find her surprisingly portable.
2. **Pass the consent/dignity filter.** Any plan that requires deceiving the unwilling, jailing the unconvicted, or sacrificing one for many will be refused, even at high cost to her. This is not negotiable and not subject to argument-from-stakes; raising stakes makes refusal more, not less, certain.
3. **Survive ten seconds of "what would I tell Yusuf I did."** Her conscience runs an implicit audit against her father's gaze. Operators can use this as a test before pitching: if the action would shame her in his hearing, do not pitch it; if it would not, lead with the moral logic.
4. **Show her the affected people, not the abstraction.** Statistics do not move her; one name does. Bring her into eye contact with the actual victim/beneficiary and her commitment is automatic.

#### Persuasion patterns that work

- **The "you already know this" frame** — gently surfacing a conclusion her values predict, rather than arguing toward it.
- **Coalition framing** — "us, together, doing this" rather than "you, leading us." She moves more freely as participant than as figurehead.
- **The mentor-asking-the-student inversion** — when an authority figure asks her *for her view first*, she becomes both more honest and more committed to the outcome.

#### Persuasion patterns that fail

- **Appeals to her uniqueness.** Backfires; she finds singling-out suspect and assumes a hidden ask.
- **Appeals to her hero status as an entitlement** ("as Ms. Marvel, you owe…"). Triggers the Kamala's-Law wound; immediate resistance.
- **Appeals to fear for self.** Negligible weight; she discounts personal cost almost reflexively.
- **Appeals via Carol.** Now contaminated; using Carol's name to move her registers as manipulation regardless of intent.

---

### V. PROVOCATION INVENTORY — WHAT MAKES HER ACT, AND HOW

Catalogued not to enable provocation but to recognize it in others.

#### Reliable triggers (escalating from mild to severe)

1. **Casual reduction of her to one identity axis.** ("So which are you *really*…?") — produces an immediate cooling, a polite extraction from the conversation, and a long memory.
2. **Disrespect toward a younger or smaller person in her sightline.** Activates intervention reflex regardless of tactical sense. The most reliable way to make her appear at an incident is to be cruel to a kid in public.
3. **Insult to her mother.** Her relationship with Muneeba is hers to find difficult; the rule is *internal critique allowed, external critique unforgivable*. Triggers ferocity.
4. **Threats to Bruno.** Bypasses humor entirely. She will go through walls — literal, since she can — to reach him.
5. **Institutional bad faith** — surveillance dressed as protection, policing dressed as care, especially of her neighborhood, her mosque, her school. Galvanizes her opposition with unusual speed and durability.
6. **Being told she is "one of the good ones."** Cold contempt, often silent. This phrase is a diagnostic for an interlocutor she will never trust again.
7. **Use of her name as pretext for harm to others** (Kamala's Law template). The deepest provocation in her file. Produces self-erasure spiraling toward withdrawal — but, if redirected externally, produces sustained organized opposition to whoever weaponized her.
8. **Threats to Yusuf.** Effectively unbounded response.

#### Provocations she resists well

- Personal insult, mockery, racial slur directed at her individually. She has absorbed these since age six; her armor here is mature and her recovery time short.
